</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="230"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="231"></td><td class="line-content">     The place is Gotham City. The time, 1987 -- once removed.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="232"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="233"></td><td class="line-content">     The city of Tomorrow: stark angles, creeping shadows, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="234"></td><td class="line-content">     dense, crowded, airless, a random tangle of steel and 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="235"></td><td class="line-content">     concrete, self-generating, almost subterranean in its 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="236"></td><td class="line-content">     aspect... as if hell had erupted through the sidewalks and 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="237"></td><td class="line-content">     kept on growing. A dangling fat moon shines overhead, ready 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="238"></td><td class="line-content">     to burst.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="239"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="240"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>EXT. CATHEDRAL - NIGHT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="241"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="242"></td><td class="line-content">     Amid the chrome and glass sits a dark and ornate Gothic 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="243"></td><td class="line-content">     anomaly: old City Cathedral, once grand, now abandoned -- 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="244"></td><td class="line-content">     long since boarded up and scheduled for demolition.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="245"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="246"></td><td class="line-content">     On the rooftop far above us, STONE GARGOYLES gaze down from 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="247"></td><td class="line-content">     their shadowy, windswept perches, keeping monstrous watch 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="248"></td><td class="line-content">     over the distant streets below, sightless guardians of the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="249"></td><td class="line-content">     Gotham night.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="250"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="251"></td><td class="line-content">     One of them is moving.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="252"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="253"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>EXT. GOTHAM SQUARE - NIGHT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="254"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="255"></td><td class="line-content">     The pulsing heart of downtown Gotham, a neon nightmare of 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="256"></td><td class="line-content">     big-city corruption, almost surreal in its oppressiveness. 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="257"></td><td class="line-content">     Hookers wave to drug dealers. Street hustlers slap high-
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="258"></td><td class="line-content">     fives with three-card monte dealers. They all seem to <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>know<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="259"></td><td class="line-content">     each other... with one conspicuous exception:
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="260"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="261"></td><td class="line-content">     A TOURIST FAMILY, Mom, Dad, and little Jimmy, staring 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="262"></td><td class="line-content">     straight  ahead as they march in perfect lockstep down the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="263"></td><td class="line-content">     main drag. They've just come out of a bit show two blocks 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="264"></td><td class="line-content">     over; the respectable theatre crowd has thinned out, and

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="266"></td><td class="line-content">     the predatory traffic of Gotham's meanest street.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="267"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="268"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              MOM
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="269"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               For God's sake, Harold, can we

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="420"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               My brother's a priest, man.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="421"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="422"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              NICK
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="423"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               No wonder you're such a chickenshit.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="424"></td><td class="line-content">               Now <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>shut up<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="425"></td><td class="line-content">                     (conclusively)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="426"></td><td class="line-content">               There ain't no bat.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="427"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="428"></td><td class="line-content">     As they speak our attention shifts to a point at the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="429"></td><td class="line-content">     opposite corner of the roof, some fifteen yards away... 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="430"></td><td class="line-content">     where, at the end of a line, a STRANGE BLACK SILHOUETTE is 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="431"></td><td class="line-content">     dropping slowly, implacably, into frame... 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="432"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="433"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              EDDIE
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="434"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               You shouldn'ta turned the gun on
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="435"></td><td class="line-content">               that kid, man. You shouldn'ta --
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="436"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="437"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              NICK
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="438"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Do you want this money or <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>don't<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="439"></td><td class="line-content">               you? Now shut up! Shut <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>up<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span> --
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="440"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="441"></td><td class="line-content">     BOTH PUNKS FREEZE at the sudden, inexplicable sound of 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="442"></td><td class="line-content">     BOOTS CRUNCHING ON GRAVEL. They turn slowly. Their JAWS 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="443"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>     DROP.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="444"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="445"></td><td class="line-content">     Standing at the edge of the roof, bathed in moonlight, is a 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="446"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>     BLACK APPARITION. IT DOES NOT MOVE.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="447"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="448"></td><td class="line-content">     EDDIE stands rooted to the spot, a choked gurgle in his 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="449"></td><td class="line-content">     throat, as if he's just seen his own death. The BLACK 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="450"></td><td class="line-content">     FIGURE advances, spreading  its arms. Or rather, its WINGS: 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="451"></td><td class="line-content">     GREAT BLACK BATWINGS, flapping in the wind.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="452"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="453"></td><td class="line-content">     NICK drops to the gravel, gropes for the gun, brings it up.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="454"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="455"></td><td class="line-content">     And still the BLACK FIGURE draws closer, deliberate, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="456"></td><td class="line-content">     menacing. On its chest: THE EMBLEM OF A BAT, in an oval 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="457"></td><td class="line-content">     yellow field, glowing like a target in the darkness... 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="458"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="459"></td><td class="line-content">     NICK FIRES TWICE. TWO CLEAN HITS. The strange black figure 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="460"></td><td class="line-content">     is knocked bodily to the roof.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="461"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="462"></td><td class="line-content">     Trembling, sweating buckets, NICK gets to his feet. He 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="463"></td><td class="line-content">     whacks a motionless EDDIE on the arm --
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="464"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="465"></td><td class="line-content">                              NICK (cont.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="466"></td><td class="line-content">               I'm gettin' outta here.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="467"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="468"></td><td class="line-content">     -- and bends to retrieve his loot. EDDIE lets out a 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="469"></td><td class="line-content">     strange, pre-verbal squeal... 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="470"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="471"></td><td class="line-content">     ... and NICK sees THE HUMAN BAT, BACK ON ITS FEET, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="472"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>     NIGHTMARISH, UNDEAD, MOVING SLOWLY AND INEVITABLY CLOSER.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="473"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="474"></td><td class="line-content">     Panic. Sheer, raw, unrelenting panic. Stolen money flutters 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="475"></td><td class="line-content">     out of NICK's hands. He scuttles around the periphery of 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="476"></td><td class="line-content">     the roof, his feet skidding on the gravel as he searches 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="477"></td><td class="line-content">     for a way down. The BLACK SPECTRE is blocking his path to 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="478"></td><td class="line-content">     the fire escape. Trapped like a rat, NICK FIRES WILDLY.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="479"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="480"></td><td class="line-content">     EDDIE is frozen in place, his eyes glazed over, his face 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="481"></td><td class="line-content">     drained of blood. The BAT treads calmly past. A LEG snakes 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="482"></td><td class="line-content">     out. A BLACK BOOT catches EDDIE high on the chest --
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="483"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="484"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>     -- LIFTS HIM CLEANLY OFF HIS FEET --
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="485"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="486"></td><td class="line-content">     -- AND SENDS HIM FLYING THROUGH THE AIR. EDDIE slams into a 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="487"></td><td class="line-content">     brick chimney and slumps to the roof unconscious, a broken, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="488"></td><td class="line-content">     weightless puppet.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="489"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="490"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>     THIS ACTION IS SO SMOOTH, SO AUTOMATIC, THAT THE BAT DOES 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="491"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>     NOT EVEN BREAK HIS STRIDE. NICK sees his chance and CHARGES 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="492"></td><td class="line-content">     past the black wraith, scrambling toward the fire escape... 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="493"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="494"></td><td class="line-content">     A GLOVED HAND slices through the air, and NICK pitches 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="495"></td><td class="line-content">     forward, his legs ensnared in a tangle of WIRES. Screaming 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="496"></td><td class="line-content">     now, he drags himself across the gravel roof, the looming 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="497"></td><td class="line-content">     figure of the BAT at his heels... 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="498"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="499"></td><td class="line-content">     ... until there's no place left to go. NICK cowers against 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="500"></td><td class="line-content">     the ledge, his pants torn, his hands and knees bloody. He 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="501"></td><td class="line-content">     has dissolved into total mindless hysteria.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="502"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="503"></td><td class="line-content">     Almost by reflex, NICK keeps shooting. He'd do better if he 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="504"></td><td class="line-content">     could manage to open his eyes. By now the hammer is falling 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="505"></td><td class="line-content">     on an empty chamber, but NICK continues, obsessively, to 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="506"></td><td class="line-content">     pull the trigger. He weeps; he moans; he wails... 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="507"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="508"></td><td class="line-content">     THE BAT grabs a fistful of NICK's shirt, and with 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="509"></td><td class="line-content">     supernatural ease HOISTS HIM into the air.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="510"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="511"></td><td class="line-content">                              NICK (cont.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="512"></td><td class="line-content">               Don't kill me... don't kill me... 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="513"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="514"></td><td class="line-content">     When NICK finally opens his eyes, he realizes THE BAT is 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="515"></td><td class="line-content">     standing on the ledge of the roof -- HOLDING HIM OUT, at 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="516"></td><td class="line-content">     arm's length, over six stories of nothingness.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="517"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="518"></td><td class="line-content">     The gruesome black apparition speaks, in a rasping whisper:
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="519"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="520"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              BATMAN
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="521"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               I won't kill you. I want you to do
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="522"></td><td class="line-content">               me a favor.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="523"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="524"></td><td class="line-content">     NICK looks down. Far, far below, CARS wink silently past.

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="527"></td><td class="line-content">     BATMAN's eyes should be, the twin reflections of his own 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="528"></td><td class="line-content">     stricken face.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="529"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="530"></td><td class="line-content">                              BATMAN (cont.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="531"></td><td class="line-content">               Tell your friends. Tell all your
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="532"></td><td class="line-content">               friends.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="533"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="534"></td><td class="line-content">     NICK HOWLS. Almost as an afterthought, THE BATMAN heaves 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="535"></td><td class="line-content">     him roughly back onto the roof. And then -- casually, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="536"></td><td class="line-content">     without a moment's hesitation -- STEPS OFF THE LEDGE OF THE 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="537"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>     ROOF, INTO MIDAIR.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="538"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="539"></td><td class="line-content">     Trembling, NICK crawls to the ledge and looks over... 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="540"></td><td class="line-content">     finding ABSOLUTELY NO TRACE of the Batman.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="541"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="542"></td><td class="line-content">     NICK is still screaming as we PAN UP to the bilious yellow 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="543"></td><td class="line-content">     globe of Gotham's moon. MAIN CREDITS ROLL:
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="544"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="545"></td><td class="line-content">                              <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>BATMAN<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="546"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="547"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                                                 CUT TO:
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="548"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="549"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. GOTHAM CITY DEMOCRATS' CLUB - NIGHT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="550"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="551"></td><td class="line-content">     An oversized CAMPAIGN POSTER fills one wall: "A NEW GOTHAM. 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="552"></td><td class="line-content">     HARVEY DENT FOR DISTRICT ATTORNEY". We TILT DOWN to find 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="553"></td><td class="line-content">     the man himself, determined, dynamic HARVEY DENT, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="554"></td><td class="line-content">     addressing a crowd from behind his podium.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="555"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="556"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              DENT
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="557"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               ... it is no longer enough to go
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="558"></td><td class="line-content">               after the small-time punks and petty
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="559"></td><td class="line-content">               criminals who infest the streets of
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="560"></td><td class="line-content">               Gotham City. Crime and corruption
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="561"></td><td class="line-content">               must be attacked at the root!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="562"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="563"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>ANOTHER ANGLE - THE AUDIENCE<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="564"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="565"></td><td class="line-content">     Civic-minded politicos decked out in fund-raiser finery. 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="566"></td><td class="line-content">     They applaud DENT's tough talk wildly. They've just shelled 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="567"></td><td class="line-content">     out $500 a plate for a chicken dinner, and by God they're 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="568"></td><td class="line-content">     going to <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>enjoy<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span> this.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="569"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="570"></td><td class="line-content">     Tuxedoed WAITERS move among the tables, deftly refilling 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="571"></td><td class="line-content">     water glasses. As they do, we SEE an EMPTY PLACE SETTING -- 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="572"></td><td class="line-content">     the only one in the hall. Some well-meaning moneybags has 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="573"></td><td class="line-content">     laid out half a grand and then neglected to show up.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="574"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="575"></td><td class="line-content">     The engraved placecard reads: BRUCE WAYNE.

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="577"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>ANGLE ON DENT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="578"></td><td class="line-content">

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="582"></td><td class="line-content">               indictment against <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>Boss Carl<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="583"></td><td class="line-content">               <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>Grissom<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>!

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="586"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="587"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. APARTMENT - NIGHT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="588"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="589"></td><td class="line-content">     A woman's apartment, decorated in pastel pinks and mauves. 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="590"></td><td class="line-content">     Original paintings and sculptures everywhere. The place 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="591"></td><td class="line-content">     reeks of money.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="592"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="593"></td><td class="line-content">     In the foreground: a MAN'S HAND, long, elegant, manicured.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="594"></td><td class="line-content">     Manipulating a DECK OF CARDS, doing a one-handed shuffle 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="595"></td><td class="line-content">     with extraordinary finesse.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="596"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="597"></td><td class="line-content">     In the background: a TV set tuned to the 11 o'clock news, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="598"></td><td class="line-content">     with highlights of HARVEY DENT's campaign speech.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="599"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="600"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              DENT
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="601"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>                     (on the TV screen)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="602"></td><td class="line-content">               Together we can make Gotham city a
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="603"></td><td class="line-content">               safe place for decent people to live
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="604"></td><td class="line-content">               and work and play.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="605"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="606"></td><td class="line-content">     THE HAND sets the deck on an end table, raps it twice, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="607"></td><td class="line-content">     turns up four aces off the top. This most unusual deck 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="608"></td><td class="line-content">     sports a .22 calibre BULLET HOLE straight through the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="609"></td><td class="line-content">     middle.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="610"></td><td class="line-content">

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="616"></td><td class="line-content">     JACK NAPIER, 32, is right-hand man and chief enforcer to

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="618"></td><td class="line-content">     feminine, and he takes a vain, gangsterish pride in his

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="623"></td><td class="line-content">     over in her negligee and snuggles up.

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1556"></td><td class="line-content">               Napier... will answer to me.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1557"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1558"></td><td class="line-content">     ECKHARDT tries to slink off. GORDON grabs him roughly.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1559"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1560"></td><td class="line-content">                              GORDON (cont.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1561"></td><td class="line-content">               You. Stick around.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1562"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1563"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. ACE CHEMICAL - THAT MOMENT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1564"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1565"></td><td class="line-content">     JACK and his HOODS ducking out of the office. It's two 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1566"></td><td class="line-content">     stories above the refinery floor, accessible by a network 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1567"></td><td class="line-content">     of steel ladders and CATWALKS running between the walls.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1568"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1569"></td><td class="line-content">     Down below, a CORRUGATED METAL DOOR begins to rise.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1570"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1571"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              COP
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1572"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Freeze!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1573"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1574"></td><td class="line-content">     One hood goes into a crouch and OPENS FIRE. Half of his 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1575"></td><td class="line-content">     colleagues dive back into the office, looking for a rear 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1576"></td><td class="line-content">     exit. The others take off across the CATWALKS.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1577"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1578"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>ANGLE ON GORDON<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1579"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1580"></td><td class="line-content">     standing in the doorway as his MEN rush into the building 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1581"></td><td class="line-content">     and take their places behind heavy machinery. SHOTS RING 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1582"></td><td class="line-content">     OUT as the HOODS scatter.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1583"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1584"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              ECKHARDT
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1585"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>                     (snidely)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1586"></td><td class="line-content">               Nice work, Commissioner.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1587"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1588"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              GORDON
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1589"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               I'm in charge here. Not Carl
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1590"></td><td class="line-content">               Grissom.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1591"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1592"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. HALLWAY - THAT MOMENT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1593"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1594"></td><td class="line-content">     TWO HOODS run down a tiled corridor in the office section 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1595"></td><td class="line-content">     of the complex. They're almost at the end of the hall when 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1596"></td><td class="line-content">     a CAPED BLACK SHADOW steps into their path.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1597"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1598"></td><td class="line-content">     It stands there, motionless. EXTENDS ITS ARMS -- like giant 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1599"></td><td class="line-content">     WINGS -- revealing the yellow-and-black insigne on its 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1600"></td><td class="line-content">     massive chest. BATMAN.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1601"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1602"></td><td class="line-content">     One millisecond later, the shocked HOODS are racing back in 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1603"></td><td class="line-content">     the opposite direction.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1604"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1605"></td><td class="line-content">     THE BATMAN flings a handful of STEEL BALL-BEARINGS across 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1606"></td><td class="line-content">     the tiled floor. HOOD I tumbles to the floor and lands 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1607"></td><td class="line-content">     hard, losing his breath. HOOD II rolls and pulls a GUN.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1608"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1609"></td><td class="line-content">     BATMAN hurls a BOOMERANG -- its edges scalloped, like a 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1610"></td><td class="line-content">     bat's wing. HOOD II finds his gun hand PINNED TO THE WALL 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1611"></td><td class="line-content">     by the twin prongs of the BATARANG.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1612"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1613"></td><td class="line-content">     THE BATMAN strides briskly toward them, businesslike, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1614"></td><td class="line-content">     taking his time. He grabs a handful of HOOD I's hair, lifts 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1615"></td><td class="line-content">     his head off the floor, KNEES HIM IN THE FACE.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1616"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1617"></td><td class="line-content">     He turns to the petrified HOOD II. CHROME-STEEL TALONS 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1618"></td><td class="line-content">     spring out of his fingertips. He strolls past HOOD II,
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1619"></td><td class="line-content">     reaching out casually to give him a QUICK NICK on the chin.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1620"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1621"></td><td class="line-content">     HOOD II slumps against the wall, unconscious.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1622"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1623"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>ANGLE ON JACK<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1624"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1625"></td><td class="line-content">     down on the floor, racing along a wall, THROWING SWITCHES 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1626"></td><td class="line-content">     -- anything to create a diversion. With every switch he 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1627"></td><td class="line-content">     throws, ANOTHER GIGANTIC MACHINE roars to life. CENTRIFUGES 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1628"></td><td class="line-content">     SPIN. HUGE POLYMER EXTRUDERS spit out thick strands of 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1629"></td><td class="line-content">     plastic gunk. OVERHEAD CHEMICAL TANKS rotate into place 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1630"></td><td class="line-content">     over giant basins.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1631"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1632"></td><td class="line-content">     JACK SEES a squad of COPS on his tail, moving from machine 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1633"></td><td class="line-content">     to machine, keeping covered. He SHOOTS AND RUNS.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1634"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1635"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>ANGLE ON CATWALKS<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1636"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1637"></td><td class="line-content">     BLASTING AWAY, HOODS III and IV scuttle across the elevated 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1638"></td><td class="line-content">     walkways, keeping down, avoiding police fire. One of them 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1639"></td><td class="line-content">     starts up a vertical ladder leading to the next catwalk up.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1640"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1641"></td><td class="line-content">     BATMAN plunges past on the end of a rope. A BLACK-GLOVED 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1642"></td><td class="line-content">     HAND snatches at HOOD III's collar as he climbs and YANKS 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1643"></td><td class="line-content">     HIM CLEANLY OFF THE LADDER. They drop to the lower catwalk.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1644"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1645"></td><td class="line-content">     HOOD IV gapes. He LEVELS HIS GUN at BATMAN, who stands his 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1646"></td><td class="line-content">     ground, holding onto the rails of the catwalk for support. 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1647"></td><td class="line-content">     A bullet hits him squarely in the chest. He <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>does not fall<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1648"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1649"></td><td class="line-content">     HOOD IV turns and scrambles. BATMAN goes to his belt for a 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1650"></td><td class="line-content">     miniature SPEAR GUN. He points it at HOOD IV and FIRES... 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1651"></td><td class="line-content">     planting a BARBED HOOK in the HOOD'S LEG.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1652"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1653"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>ANGLE ON COPS<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1654"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1655"></td><td class="line-content">     staring up in utter disbelief at the action on the catwalk.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1656"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1657"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              COP
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1658"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>               LOOK!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1659"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1660"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              GORDON
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1661"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               My God... it's <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>him<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1662"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1663"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>ANGLE ON CATWALK<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1664"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1665"></td><td class="line-content">     HOOD III, on his feet now, charges BATMAN from behind. 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1666"></td><td class="line-content">     BATMAN -- not even turning to face him -- DROPS HOOD III 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1667"></td><td class="line-content">     with an ELBOW. Now he has a HOOD on either side.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1668"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1669"></td><td class="line-content">     He takes a STEEL BILLY CLUB from his belt, whips it once 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1670"></td><td class="line-content">     through the air. It telescopes out into a FOUR-FOOT STAFF.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1671"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1672"></td><td class="line-content">     Like a drum majorette from hell, he WHIRLS THE STAFF as the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1673"></td><td class="line-content">     HOODS CONVERGE on him. HOOD III takes a debilitating JAB 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1674"></td><td class="line-content">     UNDER THE JAW. BATMAN SPINS on his heels and SLAMS THE 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1675"></td><td class="line-content">     STAFF into HOOD IV's BACK -- knocking him OFF THE CATWALK 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1676"></td><td class="line-content">     to the factory floor forty feet below!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1677"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1678"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. ACE LOADING BAY - THAT MOMENT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1679"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1680"></td><td class="line-content">     JACK spots a possible out. He hits a button on the wall; 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1681"></td><td class="line-content">     STEEL DOORS RISE to reveal ACE CARGO TRUCKS in the parking 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1682"></td><td class="line-content">     lot outside. Beyond the trucks... AN ARMY OF COPS waiting 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1683"></td><td class="line-content">     for JACK to make his move.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1684"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1685"></td><td class="line-content">     No go. He turns. Behind him, other cops -- the inside team 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1686"></td><td class="line-content">     -- are rushing at him in full riot gear. JACK ducks behind 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1687"></td><td class="line-content">     a forklift and darts into the adjacent room.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1688"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1689"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. CHEMICAL SUPPLY ROOM - A MOMENT LATER<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1690"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1691"></td><td class="line-content">     JACK sprints through the room, firing FOUR SHOTS at the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1692"></td><td class="line-content">     metal CHEMICAL TANKS on the wall. TOXIC CHEMICALS gush out 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1693"></td><td class="line-content">     onto the floor in streams. The streams run together... 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1694"></td><td class="line-content">     begin to SMOKE and SIZZLE.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1695"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1696"></td><td class="line-content">     COPS RIGHT BEHIND HIM. JACK can't resist taking one last 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1697"></td><td class="line-content">     pot-shot at a FIFTH CHEMICAL TANK.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1698"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1699"></td><td class="line-content">     AN EXPLOSION knocks him off his feet.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1700"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1701"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. FACTORY FLOOR - A MOMENT LATER<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1702"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1703"></td><td class="line-content">     COPS LOOK ON IN PUZZLEMENT as a RIVER OF CHEMICALS courses 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1704"></td><td class="line-content">     out into the main refinery. A second later, they go UP IN 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1705"></td><td class="line-content">     FLAMES. A WALL OF FIRE bisects the factory floor.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1706"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1707"></td><td class="line-content">     JACK RACES ALONG behind the spreading wall of flame. The 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1708"></td><td class="line-content">     cops can't see him now. He ducks behind a huge machine, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1709"></td><td class="line-content">     hits a switch -- and SLUICE GATES OPEN. CHEMICAL SLUDGE 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1710"></td><td class="line-content">     begins to churn. A big HOLE IN THE WALL appears as a gate 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1711"></td><td class="line-content">     opens on the East River. It's the waste dump!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1712"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1713"></td><td class="line-content">     Up on the catwalk, BATMAN has a perfect view of JACK. If 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1714"></td><td class="line-content">     JACK can just sprint through the flames without getting 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1715"></td><td class="line-content">     shot, he'll make it to the river. BATMAN hooks a rope to 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1716"></td><td class="line-content">     his Batarang, FLINGS IT at a catwalk across the floor.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1717"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1718"></td><td class="line-content">     JACK bolts. BURSTS THROUGH the wall of fire. And just as he 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1719"></td><td class="line-content">     does --
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1720"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1721"></td><td class="line-content">     BATMAN leaps off the catwalk and swings down toward him! 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1722"></td><td class="line-content">     His foot catches a THIRTY-FOOT ROLL of plastic, six feet in 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1723"></td><td class="line-content">     diameter, one of several standing upright on the floor. The 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1724"></td><td class="line-content">     plastic roll DROPS into JACK's path, BLOCKING HIS EXIT.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1725"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1726"></td><td class="line-content">     An instant later, BATMAN lands on top of JACK. Wraps an arm 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1727"></td><td class="line-content">     around his throat and RAISES his free hand. DRUG-TIPPED 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1728"></td><td class="line-content">     STEEL TALONS appear. But before he can paralyze JACK... 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1729"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1730"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              VOICE
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1731"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>               HOLD IT!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1732"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1733"></td><td class="line-content">     In all the ruckus, HOOD V has managed to circle back behind 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1734"></td><td class="line-content">     the heavy machinery. Now he's got a GUN pointed DIRECTLY AT 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1735"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>     COMMISSIONER GORDON'S HEAD.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1736"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1737"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              HOOD V
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1738"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Let him go or I'll do it.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1739"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1740"></td><td class="line-content">     BATMAN releases JACK and stands back. JACK chuckles to 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1741"></td><td class="line-content">     himself: what loyalty. Then, with plenty of time, he 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1742"></td><td class="line-content">     strolls across the floor to a Jacob's ladder mounted on the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1743"></td><td class="line-content">     back wall... and BEGINS TO CLIMB toward the catwalks.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1744"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1745"></td><td class="line-content">     All action stops. BATMAN doesn't move. The COPS don't move. 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1746"></td><td class="line-content">     HOOD V stands there sweating, his gun hand shaking as he 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1747"></td><td class="line-content">     waits for JACK to climb safely out of shooting range.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1748"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1749"></td><td class="line-content">     ECKHARDT's pig-like eyes glisten. His hand drops to his 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1750"></td><td class="line-content">     side. He's half-tempted to pull a gun and get the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1751"></td><td class="line-content">     Commissioner <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>plugged<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1752"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1753"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>ANGLE ON JACK<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1754"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1755"></td><td class="line-content">     at a crouch, groping his way along the rail of the catwalk. 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1756"></td><td class="line-content">     He reaches a paneled glass window propped open by a 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1757"></td><td class="line-content">     supporting rod. It's a forty-foot drop to the swirling 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1758"></td><td class="line-content">     black currents of the East River... and freedom.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1759"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1760"></td><td class="line-content">     He's about to climb out when his eye falls on a .38 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1761"></td><td class="line-content">     AUTOMATIC -- which lies, abandoned, on the gridwork floor 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1762"></td><td class="line-content">     of the catwalk mere yards away.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1763"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1764"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>ANGLE ON FACTORY FLOOR<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1765"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1766"></td><td class="line-content">     The HOOD, one arm around GORDON. With his gun at the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1767"></td><td class="line-content">     Commissioner's temple, he backs slowly toward the door.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1768"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1769"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              HOOD V
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1770"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Nobody makes a move. We go out
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1771"></td><td class="line-content">               clean.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1772"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1773"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              JACK'S VOICE
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1774"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>               ECKHARDT!!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1775"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1776"></td><td class="line-content">     ALL EYES TURN to the catwalk overhead, where JACK stands 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1777"></td><td class="line-content">     poised with the .38 in his fist. A SINGLE SHOT drops 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1778"></td><td class="line-content">     ECKHARDT cleanly.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1779"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1780"></td><td class="line-content">     The moment's distraction is all BATMAN needs. He hurls a 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1781"></td><td class="line-content">     NINJA WHEEL -- a small, ratcheted, razor-sharp disc -- at 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1782"></td><td class="line-content">     the FOREARM of HOOD V. One jerk of a thin filament WIRE -- 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1783"></td><td class="line-content">     a sudden SHRIEK -- and GORDON IS FREE.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1784"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1785"></td><td class="line-content">     The THUG lurches forward. His GUN DROPS to the floor, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1786"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>     DISCHARGING ACCIDENTALLY.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1787"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1788"></td><td class="line-content">     AN UNGODLY HOWL OF PAIN echoes out from the catwalk above. 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1789"></td><td class="line-content">     JACK REELS and STAGGERS, his hands CLUTCHING AT HIS CHEEKS. 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1790"></td><td class="line-content">     BLOOD GUSHES from between his fingers.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1791"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1792"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>JACK NAPIER HAS BEEN SHOT THROUGH THE FACE<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1793"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1794"></td><td class="line-content">     A YOUNG COP, unnerved by the sight of JACK's agonized 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1795"></td><td class="line-content">     pirouette, draws his gun and OPENS FIRE.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1796"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1797"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              GORDON
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1798"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>               NO!!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1799"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1800"></td><td class="line-content">     But the bullet has caught JACK in the arm. He spins, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1801"></td><td class="line-content">     totters to the edge of the catwalk... and TOPPLES OVER. The 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1802"></td><td class="line-content">     COPS look on helplessly as JACK plunges TWO STORIES DOWN 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1803"></td><td class="line-content">     into a CATCH BASIN full of BUBBLING TOXIC WASTE, SCREAMING 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1804"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>     ALL THE WAY.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1805"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1806"></td><td class="line-content">                              GORDON (cont.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1807"></td><td class="line-content">               Goddammit, we <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>had<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span> him. We --
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1808"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1809"></td><td class="line-content">     And suddenly, with JACK out of the picture, all attention 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1810"></td><td class="line-content">     focusses on THE BATMAN. COPS reach for their guns, circle 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1811"></td><td class="line-content">     warily around him. Cornered now, he backs off slowly, HANDS 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1812"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>     ON HIS BELT.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1813"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1814"></td><td class="line-content">                              GORDON (cont.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1815"></td><td class="line-content">               Hold it right there, Mister.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1816"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1817"></td><td class="line-content">     THE BATMAN raises his hands in a gesture of surrender. Then 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1818"></td><td class="line-content">     -- as the COPS advance -- he flicks TWO TINY CAPSULES onto 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1819"></td><td class="line-content">     the factory floor.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1820"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1821"></td><td class="line-content">     A BLINDING FLASH OF LIGHT. COLORS BURST in a wild 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1822"></td><td class="line-content">     pyrotechnic display. COPS stumble backwards, momentarily 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1823"></td><td class="line-content">     dazzled, as a THICK WALL OF BLACK SMOKE conceals BATMAN 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1824"></td><td class="line-content">     from view.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1825"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1826"></td><td class="line-content">     A TINY GRAPPLING HOOK rockets out of the dense curling 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1827"></td><td class="line-content">     cloud and CATCHES on a catwalk overhead.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1828"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1829"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              COP
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1830"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>               LOOK!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1831"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1832"></td><td class="line-content">     The COPS are firing wildly into the smoke. But it's too 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1833"></td><td class="line-content">     late. At the end of a cord, THE BLACK MAJESTIC FIGURE OF 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1834"></td><td class="line-content">     THE BATMAN whips upward, rising out of the smoke like an 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1835"></td><td class="line-content">     avenging angel -- and DISAPPEARING into the shadowy 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1836"></td><td class="line-content">     heights, safely out of range.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1837"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1838"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              GORDON
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1839"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>               HOLD YOUR FIRE!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1840"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1841"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              COP
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1842"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               ... Who <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>is<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span> this guy?
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1843"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1844"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              GORDON

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1850"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>EXT. ACE CHEMICAL CO. - THAT MOMENT - NIGHT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1852"></td><td class="line-content">     A BLACK SHADOW scurries across the roof. From the

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1855"></td><td class="line-content">     deck, pierced by a neat, round bullet hole, bobbing on the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1856"></td><td class="line-content">     oily surface of the foul, polluted river.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1857"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1858"></td><td class="line-content">     As deadly toxins gush forth, OTHER CARDS from the deck

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2292"></td><td class="line-content">     hair, and so it's a moment before he sees the bundled-up
