</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2294"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2295"></td><td class="line-content">                              GRISSOM (cont.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2296"></td><td class="line-content">               Who the hell are you?
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2297"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2298"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              JACK
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2299"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               It's me. "Sugar Bumps."
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2300"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2301"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              GRISSOM
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2302"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>                     (recognizing his voice)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2303"></td><td class="line-content">               Jack?
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2304"></td><td class="line-content">                     (advancing cautiously)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2305"></td><td class="line-content">               Thank God. I can't believe it's you.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2306"></td><td class="line-content">               I heard you'd been --
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2307"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2308"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              JACK
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2309"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>                     (standing up)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2310"></td><td class="line-content">               Is that what you "heard"?
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2311"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2312"></td><td class="line-content">     JACK gestures him over to the empty chair. GRISSOM doesn't 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2313"></td><td class="line-content">     move until he sees the GUN pointed at his belly.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2314"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2315"></td><td class="line-content">                              JACK (cont.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2316"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>               YOU SET ME UP!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2317"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>                     (beat)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2318"></td><td class="line-content">               Over a <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>girl<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>. You must be insane!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2319"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2320"></td><td class="line-content">     GRISSOM surreptitiously reaches for a desk drawer.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2321"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2322"></td><td class="line-content">                              JACK (cont.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2323"></td><td class="line-content">               Keep your hands on the desk.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2324"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2325"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              GRISSOM
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2326"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Sooner or later you would've tried
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2327"></td><td class="line-content">               to take me, Jack. You may get me
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2328"></td><td class="line-content">               now, but your life won't be worth a
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2329"></td><td class="line-content">               dime.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2330"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2331"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              JACK
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2332"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               I've died once already. It wasn't so
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2333"></td><td class="line-content">               bad. -- In fact I <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>recommend<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span> it.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2334"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2335"></td><td class="line-content">     GRISSOM is beginning to panic now. It's obvious that JACK 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2336"></td><td class="line-content">     is utterly, hopelessly deranged.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2337"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2338"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              GRISSOM
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2339"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Jack, listen -- we'll cut a deal --
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2340"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2341"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              JACK
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2342"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>               JACK? JACK? DO I LOOK LIKE A JACK??
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2343"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2344"></td><td class="line-content">     And now, for the first time, he flings away the hat. RIPS 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2345"></td><td class="line-content">     THE MUFFLER from his face. And -- as GRISSOM gasps in shock 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2346"></td><td class="line-content">     -- STANDS REVEALED in his full horrendous glory.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2347"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2348"></td><td class="line-content">     His flesh is bleached bone-white. His hair is a luminous 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2349"></td><td class="line-content">     seaweed-green. And his cheeks are torn and puckered from 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2350"></td><td class="line-content">     the bullet wound, TWISTING HIS MOUTH INTO A HIDEOUS, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2351"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>     PERPETUAL HARLEQUIN'S GRIN.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2352"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2353"></td><td class="line-content">                              JACK (cont.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2354"></td><td class="line-content">               I'm not a Jack any more.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2355"></td><td class="line-content">                     (pause; cackling)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2356"></td><td class="line-content">               You made me a Joker!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2357"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2358"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>     THE CACKLE BUILDS INTO FURIOUS, HYSTERICAL LAUGHTER. 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2359"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>     GRISSOM, revulsed, terrified, pushes himself away from the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2360"></td><td class="line-content">     desk, back toward the window which overlooks the city.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2361"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2362"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              GRISSOM
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2363"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Jack -- I'm warning you. WIPE THAT
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2364"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>               LUNATIC GRIN OFF YOUR FACE.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2365"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2366"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              JACK
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2367"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               HA! That's the best part. I CAN'T!!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2368"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2369"></td><td class="line-content">     And with that JACK pulls the trigger. And fires. And fires 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2370"></td><td class="line-content">     again until the CLIP IS EMPTY.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2371"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2372"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>EXT. GRISSOM'S BUILDING - NIGHT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2373"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2374"></td><td class="line-content">     We TILT UP the chrome-and-glass facade of the skyscraper, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2375"></td><td class="line-content">     arriving finally at the TOP FLOOR: a PLATE GLASS WINDOW 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2376"></td><td class="line-content">     spiderwebbed with cracks where Jack's bullets hit.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2377"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2378"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. GRISSOM'S PENTHOUSE - THAT MOMENT - NIGHT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2379"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2380"></td><td class="line-content">     The room is still dark. JACK -- or, as we'll know him from 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2381"></td><td class="line-content">     this moment on, THE JOKER -- sits in GRISSOM's swivel 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2382"></td><td class="line-content">     chair, staring out at the moon-drenched skyline.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2383"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2384"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              JOKER
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2385"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               What a view. Our little city. It
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2386"></td><td class="line-content">               always brings a smile to my face.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2387"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2388"></td><td class="line-content">     He reaches for a nearby glass of liquor and glances down at 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2389"></td><td class="line-content">     GRISSOM -- who lies dead on the floor, the towel still 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2390"></td><td class="line-content">     wrapped around him. THE JOKER laughs softly to himself.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2391"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2392"></td><td class="line-content">                              JOKER (cont.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2393"></td><td class="line-content">               Guess it's <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>my<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span> little city now.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2394"></td><td class="line-content">               Wonder what it'll look like when I
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2395"></td><td class="line-content">               get done with it.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2396"></td><td class="line-content">                     (pause)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2397"></td><td class="line-content">               I bet it'll be something real fine.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2398"></td><td class="line-content">               <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>Real fine and pretty<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>.

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2402"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. BRUCE WAYNE'S BEDROOM - MORNING<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2403"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2404"></td><td class="line-content">     The sun is just up, and VICKI finds herself alone in bed. A 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2405"></td><td class="line-content">     SOFT, OFF-KEY BARITONE VOICE drifts out of the adjacent 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2406"></td><td class="line-content">     bathroom: BRUCE in the shower, singing "Honeysuckle Rose."
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2407"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2408"></td><td class="line-content">     She breaks into a huge smile and climbs out of bed. Somehow 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2409"></td><td class="line-content">     she's wound up wearing BRUCE's ribbed formal shirt.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2410"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2411"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. BATHROOM - A MOMENT LATER - MORNING<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2412"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2413"></td><td class="line-content">     BRUCE in his opulent deco shower stall, still SINGING to 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2414"></td><td class="line-content">     himself. VICKI sneaks up behind him, opens the door. He 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2415"></td><td class="line-content">     instantly STOPS SINGING -- as if he's been hit by a brick.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2416"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2417"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              VICKI
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2418"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               I didn't mean to scare you. I just
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2419"></td><td class="line-content">               had to come in here and see it that
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2420"></td><td class="line-content">               was really you <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>singing<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>.

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2422"></td><td class="line-content">     She smiles, teasing him. He doesn't respond. He acts as if 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2423"></td><td class="line-content">     she's caught him doing something shameful -- <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>exposed<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span> him.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2424"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2425"></td><td class="line-content">                              VICKI (cont.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2426"></td><td class="line-content">                     (singing)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2427"></td><td class="line-content">               "Don't buy sugar -- you just have to

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2430"></td><td class="line-content">                     (no response from BRUCE)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2431"></td><td class="line-content">               Bruce, you are such a case.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2432"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2433"></td><td class="line-content">     BRUCE seems somehow unable to sing along. But be quickly

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2435"></td><td class="line-content">     childish smile.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2436"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2437"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              BRUCE
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2438"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               I don't sing very well.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2439"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2440"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              VICKI
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2441"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Then there's one thing in the world
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2442"></td><td class="line-content">               you don't do very well. And I know
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2443"></td><td class="line-content">               what it is. -- Now you'll have to
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2444"></td><td class="line-content">               kill me.

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2446"></td><td class="line-content">     He kisses her good morning, steps out and reaches for a 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2447"></td><td class="line-content">     towel. His body is one big mass of BRUISES AND ABRASIONS.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2448"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2449"></td><td class="line-content">                              VICKI (cont.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2450"></td><td class="line-content">               Poor thing. You should stay off that
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2451"></td><td class="line-content">               horse.

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2453"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                                                   CUT TO:
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2454"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2455"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. GLOBE - CITY ROOM - DAY<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2456"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2457"></td><td class="line-content">     KNOX, in a surly mood, examines the morning edition of the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2458"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>Globe<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>. He's turned to page six -- the gossip page -- and 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2459"></td><td class="line-content">     there, under Miranda Reitz's byline, is a picture of VICKI. 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2460"></td><td class="line-content">     It seems she and BRUCE are the talk of the town.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2461"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2462"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              KNOX
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2463"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>                     (disgusted)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2464"></td><td class="line-content">               ...Peanut.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2465"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2466"></td><td class="line-content">     A COPY BOY approaches his desk with a MANILA FOLDER:
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2467"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2468"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              COPY BOY
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2469"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Here's that morgue file you wanted.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2470"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2471"></td><td class="line-content">     KNOX leans back in his chair. The file is labelled "BRUCE 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2472"></td><td class="line-content">     WAYNE: 1982-1987."  KNOX opens it and begins to leaf 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2473"></td><td class="line-content">     through old clippings from back issues of the <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>Globe<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2474"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2475"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>     WAYNE FOUNDATION TO FUND LOW-COST HOUSING. MILLIONAIRE 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2476"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>     HEADS CHARITY DRIVE FOR GOTHAM HANDICAPPED. HURRICANE 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2477"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>     VICTIMS SAY 'THANK YOU' TO BRUCE WAYNE. KNOX's face sags in 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2478"></td><td class="line-content">     dismay. Every article seems to be telling us just how swell 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2479"></td><td class="line-content">     a rich philanthropist can be.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2480"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2481"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              KNOX
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2482"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Come on. Gimme some <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>dirt<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>!

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2484"></td><td class="line-content">     Then he notices something odd. In the whole fat file of 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2485"></td><td class="line-content">     clippings, <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>there are no pictures of Bruce Wayne<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span> -- with two 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2486"></td><td class="line-content">     partial exceptions.

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2488"></td><td class="line-content">     One is a group shot, Bruce in the middle, waving at the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2489"></td><td class="line-content">     camera and blocking our view of his face. The other is an 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2490"></td><td class="line-content">     ancient picture of a collegiate Bruce, stern-faced, hair 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2491"></td><td class="line-content">     down to his collar. The caption reads "BRUCE WAYNE IN 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2492"></td><td class="line-content">     1973" -- years out of date even when it ran in the paper.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2493"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2494"></td><td class="line-content">                              KNOX (cont.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2495"></td><td class="line-content">               ... Why don't you like your picture

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2500"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. APARTMENT LOBBY - NIGHT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2501"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2502"></td><td class="line-content">     A DOORMAN DOZES in the plush lobby of ALICIA HUNT's 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2503"></td><td class="line-content">     apartment building on the East Side of Gotham. Through the

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2537"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. PENTHOUSE SUITE - DAY<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2655"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2656"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>EXT. HALLIDAY PLAZA - DAY<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2657"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2658"></td><td class="line-content">     A sunny, landscaped quad surrounded by corporate 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2659"></td><td class="line-content">     skyscrapers: trees, grass, marble fountains, flags of many 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2660"></td><td class="line-content">     nations. Amid the pedestrians we catch BRUCE and VICKI, all 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2661"></td><td class="line-content">     smiles, cutting through the plaza on the way to lunch.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2662"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2663"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              VICKI
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2664"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               ... To tell you the truth, I'd just
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2665"></td><td class="line-content">               about given up waiting.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2666"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2667"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              BRUCE
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2668"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               I said I'd call you the minute I got
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2669"></td><td class="line-content">               free. And I did. -- And here we are.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2670"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2671"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              VICKI
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2672"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>                     (teasing him)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2673"></td><td class="line-content">               Hm hmm. Lunch. Not even dinner.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2674"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2675"></td><td class="line-content">     He stops in his tracks, takes her by the shoulders.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2676"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2677"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              BRUCE
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2678"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Vicki. Do you want the whole truth?
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2679"></td><td class="line-content">               All coyness aside?
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2680"></td><td class="line-content">                     (long pause)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2681"></td><td class="line-content">               I wish I had more time to give you.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2682"></td><td class="line-content">               Every day I don't see you, I miss
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2683"></td><td class="line-content">               you.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2684"></td><td class="line-content">                     (beat)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2685"></td><td class="line-content">               Now. Are you going to waste this
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2686"></td><td class="line-content">               lovely afternoon being all mad at
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2687"></td><td class="line-content">               me?
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2688"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2689"></td><td class="line-content">     All this, of course, is delivered with devastating 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2690"></td><td class="line-content">     sincerity. VICKI finds herself totally disarmed.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2691"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2692"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              VICKI
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2693"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Okay, I'm a sucker. You sound so
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2694"></td><td class="line-content">               much like someone I used to... 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2695"></td><td class="line-content">                     (stopping suddenly)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2696"></td><td class="line-content">               Bruce? I know this is silly, but --
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2697"></td><td class="line-content">               you're not <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>married<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>, are you?
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2698"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2699"></td><td class="line-content">     He stops and laughs. She smiles crookedly, takes his arm.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2700"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2701"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>ANOTHER ANGLE - ACROSS PLAZA - THAT MOMENT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2702"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2703"></td><td class="line-content">     PHILLY RICORSO -- another CRIMELORD from the boardroom -- 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2704"></td><td class="line-content">     enters the plaza flanked by a cadre of PAID BODYGUARDS.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2705"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2706"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>ON BRUCE AND VICKI<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2707"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2708"></td><td class="line-content">     A PAINTED STREET MIME walks alongside them, feeling his way 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2709"></td><td class="line-content">     along an imaginary wall. VICKI groans.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2710"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2711"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              VICKI
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2712"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               All street mimes should be executed.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2713"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2714"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              BRUCE
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2715"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               ... Looks like a <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>convention<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2716"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2717"></td><td class="line-content">     And indeed, there are HALF A DOZEN STREET MIMES converging 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2718"></td><td class="line-content">     on the center of the plaza.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2719"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2720"></td><td class="line-content">     RICORSO and co. approach the mirrored-glass entrance of a 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2721"></td><td class="line-content">     skyscraper. In the lobby, A MIME -- who's been annoying the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2722"></td><td class="line-content">     passersby -- THROWS A BOLT, LOCKING THE DOORS from inside.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2723"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2724"></td><td class="line-content">     A BODYGUARD bangs on the glass. Nearby, ANOTHER MIME 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2725"></td><td class="line-content">     reaches into a trash bin -- and pulls out a MACHINE GUN.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2726"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2727"></td><td class="line-content">     SUDDEN SCREAMS OF TERROR from the onlookers.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2728"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2729"></td><td class="line-content">     VICKI turns to BRUCE. Before she can get his name out, he's 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2730"></td><td class="line-content">     HOISTED HER BODILY and THROWN HER behind a marble fountain.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2731"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2732"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>SERIES OF SHOTS<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2733"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2734"></td><td class="line-content">     BRUCE'S EYES darting birdlike around the plaza -- INTERCUT 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2735"></td><td class="line-content">     with the following POV SHOTS, ALL IN SLOW MOTION:
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2736"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2737"></td><td class="line-content">     -    TWO MIMES with machine guns. One of them lining PHILLY 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2738"></td><td class="line-content">          and co. up against the glass doors, the other holding 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2739"></td><td class="line-content">          the CROWD at bay;
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2740"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2741"></td><td class="line-content">     -    A WOMAN in the crowd fainting. A THIRD MIME gleefully 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2742"></td><td class="line-content">          imitating her swoon, to no one's amusement;
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2743"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2744"></td><td class="line-content">     -    PHILLY and his goons, COWERING, hands in the air, as 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2745"></td><td class="line-content">          OTHER MIMES cruelly mimic their terrified poses... 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2746"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2747"></td><td class="line-content">     ... and suddenly BRUCE is RUNNING FRANTICALLY, looking for 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2748"></td><td class="line-content">     a secluded spot, an alleyway, anything. No go. He's out in 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2749"></td><td class="line-content">     the open, with onlookers everywhere. In his civvies, he's 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2750"></td><td class="line-content">     just another citizen... TOTALLY IMPOTENT.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2751"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2752"></td><td class="line-content">     He darts around a corner, backs against a wall. WOMEN, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2753"></td><td class="line-content">     CHILDREN, GROWN MEN race past. <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>No privacy<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>. He's 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2754"></td><td class="line-content">     practically quaking now, in the throes of some terrible 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2755"></td><td class="line-content">     anxiety. He looks up at the sky overhead, terrified.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2756"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2757"></td><td class="line-content">     A BRILLIANT SUN bears down on him as MACHINE GUNS CHATTER.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2758"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2759"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>ANGLE ON PHILLY AND BODYGUARDS<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2760"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2761"></td><td class="line-content">     BODIES JERKING as GLASS rains down in shards.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2762"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2763"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>ANGLE ON BRUCE<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2764"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2765"></td><td class="line-content">     his back arched, his mouth agape, his face drained of blood 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2766"></td><td class="line-content">     as the sounds of carnage echo through the plaza. It's 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2767"></td><td class="line-content">     almost as if the bullets are striking <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>him<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2768"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2769"></td><td class="line-content">     A moment later, it's all over but the screaming. VICKI 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2770"></td><td class="line-content">     emerges from the crowd and finds BRUCE slumped against the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2771"></td><td class="line-content">     wall, nearly catatonic. She moves to touch him.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2772"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2773"></td><td class="line-content">     As if by reflex he reaches out and GRABS HER BY THE ARMS -- 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2774"></td><td class="line-content">     with a grip so strong it could crush bone. She GASPS, looks 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2775"></td><td class="line-content">     up -- and sees, in his traumatized EYES, a look so raw, so 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2776"></td><td class="line-content">     desperate, that it virtually defies comprehension.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2777"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2778"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              VICKI
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2779"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>               BRUCE!!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2780"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2781"></td><td class="line-content">     He blinks rapidly. He relaxes his grip. Before VICKI's 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2782"></td><td class="line-content">     eyes, he's changing... becoming the BRUCE she knows.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2783"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2784"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              BRUCE
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2785"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Oh my God... are you all right?
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2786"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2787"></td><td class="line-content">     He reaches for her. Involuntarily, she steps back.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2788"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2789"></td><td class="line-content">     He sees her reaction and his face goes slack -- frightened, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2790"></td><td class="line-content">     pleading. This time she lets him embrace her... but her 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2791"></td><td class="line-content">     face is full of bewilderment and doubt.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2792"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2793"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INSERT - TELEVISION SCREEN<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2794"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2795"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              ANCHORWOMAN
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2796"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               ... live from Halliday Plaza, where a
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2797"></td><td class="line-content">               gangland-style execution claimed the
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2798"></td><td class="line-content">               life of racketeer Philly Ricorso.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2799"></td><td class="line-content">               Ricorso's death is the third in a
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2800"></td><td class="line-content">               rash of underworld killings... 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2801"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2802"></td><td class="line-content">     CUT TO TWO-SHOT: the ANCHORWOMAN and COMMISSIONER GORDON.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2803"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2804"></td><td class="line-content">                              ANCHORWOMAN (cont.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2805"></td><td class="line-content">               Commissioner, you've heard the
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2806"></td><td class="line-content">               rumors. Are these murders the work
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2807"></td><td class="line-content">               of the mysterious 'Batman'?
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2808"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2809"></td><td class="line-content">     A PIERCING CACKLE fills the air. CAMERA PULLS BACK from the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2810"></td><td class="line-content">     TV, placing us in the JOKER's boardroom. Behind the big 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2811"></td><td class="line-content">     desk he SWIVELS INTO VIEW, phone in hand.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2812"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2813"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              JOKER
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2814"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               All <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>reet<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>! I think it's about time
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2815"></td><td class="line-content">               we called another meeting, huh?
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2816"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2817"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                                                 CUT TO:
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2818"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2819"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. WAYNE MANOR - DAY<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2820"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2821"></td><td class="line-content">     ALFRED on the phone, a feather duster in his hand.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2822"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2823"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              ALFRED
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2824"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               I'm sorry, Miss Vale. I've given him
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2825"></td><td class="line-content">               your messages. That's all I can do.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2826"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2827"></td><td class="line-content">     ANGLE WIDENS. BRUCE is sitting mere feet away, obviously 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2828"></td><td class="line-content">     distraught, locked in some sort of internal struggle.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2829"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2830"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. VICKI'S APARTMENT - THAT MOMENT - DAY<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2831"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2832"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              VICKI
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2833"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Please tell him... I'm not trying to
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2834"></td><td class="line-content">               make his life difficult. I'd just --
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2835"></td><td class="line-content">               I'd just like to know what's going
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2836"></td><td class="line-content">               <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>on<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2837"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2838"></td><td class="line-content">     A KNOCK at the door as VICKI hangs up. She goes to open it, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="2839"></td><td class="line-content">     finds KNOX -- wearing a big, cheshire-cat smile.

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3380"></td><td class="line-content">     bearing a single word: URGENT.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3381"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3382"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              WAITER
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3383"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Miss Vale, this just arrived for
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3384"></td><td class="line-content">               you.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3385"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3386"></td><td class="line-content">     As the WAITER leaves, she tears off the wrapper. Inside is 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3387"></td><td class="line-content">     a small white box and a NOTE -- SCRIBBLED IN CRAYON.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3388"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3389"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>               DEAR V. VALE,

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3392"></td><td class="line-content">     Unsigned, of course. VICKI, puzzled, opens the box to find 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3393"></td><td class="line-content">     a MINIATURE GAS MASK.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3394"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3395"></td><td class="line-content">     She hears a strange HISSING NOISE. A few feet away, GREEN 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3396"></td><td class="line-content">     SMOKE is billowing out of an air-conditioning vent.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3397"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3398"></td><td class="line-content">     TRAYS OF FOOD CRASH TO THE FLOOR as WAITERS pass out. ART 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3399"></td><td class="line-content">     LOVERS drop forks, go face down in their pasta salad.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3400"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3401"></td><td class="line-content">     VICKI hurriedly fits the gas mask over her nose and mouth. 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3402"></td><td class="line-content">     Within seconds, she's the only one conscious in the room.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3403"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3404"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. MUSEUM - THAT MOMENT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3405"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3406"></td><td class="line-content">     GREEN SMOKE plumes up toward the ceiling as we TILT DOWN 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3407"></td><td class="line-content">     toward the floor of the atrium. PATRONS and SECURITY GUARDS 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3408"></td><td class="line-content">     lie sprawled on the floor, twisted at odd angles, out cold.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3409"></td><td class="line-content">

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3411"></td><td class="line-content">     and in strolls THE JOKER, looking quite dapper in his
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3412"></td><td class="line-content">     street makeup and BIG PURPLE PIMP'S HAT.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3413"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3414"></td><td class="line-content">     A SQUAD OF GOONS enters behind him. Some of them are

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3418"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3419"></td><td class="line-content">     The JOKER steps up onto the ramp, examines the artwork with 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3420"></td><td class="line-content">     an appreciative eye.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3421"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3422"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              JOKER
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3423"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Okay, boys, let's broaden our minds.

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="3951"></td><td class="line-content">     stranded two stories up -- SITTING DUCKS.

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4305"></td><td class="line-content">     At the side of the road, a FALLEN TREE, surrounded by

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4309"></td><td class="line-content">     Doing sixty, the BATMOBILE makes a hairpin turn. Seconds 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4310"></td><td class="line-content">     later, the FALLEN TREE drops back magically into place.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4311"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4312"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. BATMOBILE - A MOMENT LATER - NIGHT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
