</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4487"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4488"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              VICKI
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4489"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               ... Bruce?
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4490"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4491"></td><td class="line-content">     HE FREEZES IN PLACE for an indecisive moment. Then:
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4492"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4493"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              BATMAN
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4494"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Are you talking to me?
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4495"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4496"></td><td class="line-content">     He turns in seeming incomprehension. And shows her a 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4497"></td><td class="line-content">     SMILE... the same crooked, curious, childlike smile she saw 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4498"></td><td class="line-content">     on BRUCE's face that morning when she caught him singing.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4499"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4500"></td><td class="line-content">                              BATMAN (cont.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4501"></td><td class="line-content">               Maybe we've had enough for one
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4502"></td><td class="line-content">               night. I'll take you home.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4503"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4504"></td><td class="line-content">     Almost in a trance now, she lets him lead her to the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4505"></td><td class="line-content">     BATMOBILE. As she takes her seat he reaches into his 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4506"></td><td class="line-content">     utility belt for another KNOCKOUT CAPSULE.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4507"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4508"></td><td class="line-content">                              BATMAN (cont.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4509"></td><td class="line-content">               Do you want to do it this time?
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4510"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4511"></td><td class="line-content">     VICKI doesn't move. She looks at the capsule in her hand as 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4512"></td><td class="line-content">     he walks over to the driver's side and gets in.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4513"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4514"></td><td class="line-content">                              BATMAN (cont.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4515"></td><td class="line-content">               Don't be afraid. I'm here.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4516"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4517"></td><td class="line-content">     She takes one last look at the familiar SMILE beneath the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4518"></td><td class="line-content">     mask... then breaks the capsule and BREATHES DEEP.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4519"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4520"></td><td class="line-content">     FLAME ERUPTS from the rear of the Batmobile as the after-
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4521"></td><td class="line-content">     burners kick in and BATMAN screeches off. A FIERY RED GLOW 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4522"></td><td class="line-content">     fills the screen, BURNING OUT THE IMAGE as we
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4523"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4524"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                                                 DISSOLVE TO:
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4525"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4526"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>EXT. GOTHAM STREET - 1963 - NIGHT (DREAM SEQUENCE)<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4527"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4528"></td><td class="line-content">     The red glow resolves itself into a DREAMLIKE STREET SCENE: 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4529"></td><td class="line-content">     liquid, weightless figures moving in a tinted, soundless 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4530"></td><td class="line-content">     cityscape as DISTANT, TINKLY CARNIVAL MUSIC plays 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4531"></td><td class="line-content">     underneath. We're outside a theatre watching first-nighters 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4532"></td><td class="line-content">     emerge from the opening of a hit musical.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4533"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4534"></td><td class="line-content">     In the crowd we pick out THREE FIGURES: DR. THOMAS WAYNE, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4535"></td><td class="line-content">     his wife MARTHA, and -- in THOMAS's arms -- their young son 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4536"></td><td class="line-content">     BRUCE. BRUCE hasn't made it through the show. He's asleep, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4537"></td><td class="line-content">     head nestled peacefully against his father's shoulder.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4538"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4539"></td><td class="line-content">     THOMAS rouses the boy gently, sets him down on the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4540"></td><td class="line-content">     sidewalk. BRUCE rubs the sleep from his eyes as THOMAS puts 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4541"></td><td class="line-content">     an arm around his wife. Together they begin walking.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4542"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4543"></td><td class="line-content">     IN A SINGLE CUT the crowd has DISAPPEARED, and the WAYNES 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4544"></td><td class="line-content">     are walking toward us up a deserted street. THOMAS and 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4545"></td><td class="line-content">     MARTHA are laughing, making jokes, reaching down to tousle 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4546"></td><td class="line-content">     BRUCE's hair. Their FACES, as they draw closer, are FULL OF 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4547"></td><td class="line-content">     JOY. And then, without warning --
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4548"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4549"></td><td class="line-content">     A HANDGUN enters frame.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4550"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4551"></td><td class="line-content">     The WAYNES freeze in their tracks. THOMAS steps 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4552"></td><td class="line-content">     protectively in front of his wife, reaches for his wallet, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4553"></td><td class="line-content">     begins unbuckling his watch. He won't put up a fight.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4554"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4555"></td><td class="line-content">     MARTHA's hand goes involuntarily to the PEARL NECKLACE at 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4556"></td><td class="line-content">     her throat.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4557"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4558"></td><td class="line-content">     The GUNMAN sees it, gestures for her to hand it over. But 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4559"></td><td class="line-content">     MARTHA is paralyzed, afraid to move.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4560"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4561"></td><td class="line-content">     The GUNMAN steps past THOMAS, SNATCHES AT THE NECKLACE.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4562"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4563"></td><td class="line-content">     The instant his wife is threatened, THOMAS ATTACKS. The 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4564"></td><td class="line-content">     pearl strand BREAKS in the GUNMAN'S HAND as he drops toward 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4565"></td><td class="line-content">     the sidewalk.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4566"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4567"></td><td class="line-content">     A SILENT BURST OF FLAME erupts from the muzzle of the gun.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4568"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4569"></td><td class="line-content">     THOMAS CRUMPLES. MARTHA emits a PIERCING SHRIEK -- a shriek 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4570"></td><td class="line-content">     we cannot hear --
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4571"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4572"></td><td class="line-content">     -- a shriek cut short by a second burst of flame.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4573"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4574"></td><td class="line-content">     BRUCE stands paralyzed in shock. THE GUNMAN scoops a 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4575"></td><td class="line-content">     handful of pearls off the sidewalk, reaches for MARTHA's 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4576"></td><td class="line-content">     purse, and rises slowly -- his gun levelled directly at the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4577"></td><td class="line-content">     boy.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4578"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4579"></td><td class="line-content">     Almost catatonic, BRUCE stares down at the corpses of his 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4580"></td><td class="line-content">     parents. At their hands, somehow intertwined. At the tiny 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4581"></td><td class="line-content">     glinting pearls and the spreading pool of blood around 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4582"></td><td class="line-content">     them.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4583"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4584"></td><td class="line-content">     He looks up with a gaze so bleak, so petrifying... that the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4585"></td><td class="line-content">     GUNMAN turns and runs.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4586"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4587"></td><td class="line-content">     AND WE CUT. To an exact reproduction of the Pulitzer Prize-
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4588"></td><td class="line-content">     winning photo... the cops bent over the bodies, the medics 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4589"></td><td class="line-content">     with their stretchers, the boy BRUCE, his arms wrapped 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4590"></td><td class="line-content">     tightly around the waist of OFFICER GORDON.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4591"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4592"></td><td class="line-content">     There's only one difference. BRUCE's head is turned away 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4593"></td><td class="line-content">     from us. <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>We can't see his face<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4594"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4595"></td><td class="line-content">     And now a HAND enters the frame. Much like the GUNMAN's 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4596"></td><td class="line-content">     hand, but feminine, beckoning. BRUCE, hearing his name, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4597"></td><td class="line-content">     LOOKS UP; then, agonized, ashamed, he BURIES HIS FACE in 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4598"></td><td class="line-content">     GORDON's side. GORDON gestures angrily at the intruder.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4599"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4600"></td><td class="line-content">     But the hand keeps beckoning. And ultimately BRUCE turns. 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4601"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>Showing us the tear-stained face from the famous photo<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>. A
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4602"></td><td class="line-content">     face slack with horror. The horror of his parents' death... 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4603"></td><td class="line-content">     and more importantly, <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>the horror that someone would dare to<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4604"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>violate this most private and terrible of moments<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4605"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4606"></td><td class="line-content">     At last we see what BRUCE sees: a WOMAN crouched on the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4607"></td><td class="line-content">     sidewalk nearby. The WOMAN is holding a camera. The WOMAN 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4608"></td><td class="line-content">     is smiling prettily at BRUCE.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4609"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4610"></td><td class="line-content">     The WOMAN is VICKI VALE.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4611"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4612"></td><td class="line-content">     A FLASHBULB EXPLODES. FILLING. THE SCREEN with its blinding 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4613"></td><td class="line-content">     white light, SCORCHING OUT THE IMAGE as a HARSH RINGING 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4614"></td><td class="line-content">     SOUND cuts through the silence.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4615"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4616"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                                                 CUT TO:
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4617"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4618"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. BEDROOM - NIGHT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4619"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4620"></td><td class="line-content">     VICKI AWAKENS. She sits up in bed, tremulous, distraught. 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4621"></td><td class="line-content">     The bedside phone is ringing. She reaches for it, but her 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4622"></td><td class="line-content">     hand freezes in midair. She knows who's calling.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4623"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4624"></td><td class="line-content">     Three rings later, she manages to lift the receiver. To her 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4625"></td><td class="line-content">     amazement, she finds she cannot speak. Finally, she hears a 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4626"></td><td class="line-content">     VOICE at the other end of the line.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4627"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4628"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              BRUCE (V.O.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4629"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Vicki... ?
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4630"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4631"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. BRUCE WAYNE'S STUDY - NIGHT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4632"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4633"></td><td class="line-content">     BRUCE at a big mahogany desk in his somber, book-lined 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4634"></td><td class="line-content">     study. The room is dark but for a small table lamp.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4635"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4636"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              BRUCE
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4637"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Vicki, I've been thinking about you.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4638"></td><td class="line-content">                     (long pause)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4639"></td><td class="line-content">               I know it's late. I'm sorry. I --
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4640"></td><td class="line-content">               Are you there?
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4641"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4642"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INTERCUT BRUCE AND VICKI<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4643"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4644"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              VICKI
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4645"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Yes, Bruce -- I'm here --
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4646"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4647"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              BRUCE
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4648"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               I'm sorry about the way things went
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4649"></td><td class="line-content">               between us. I'd very much like to
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4650"></td><td class="line-content">               see you again.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4651"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4652"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              VICKI
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4653"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Well, Bruce... I don't think... that
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4654"></td><td class="line-content">               would be possible.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4655"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4656"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              BRUCE
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4657"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               I wish you'd reconsider.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4658"></td><td class="line-content">                     (groping)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4659"></td><td class="line-content">               I didn't stand you up today. The
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4660"></td><td class="line-content">               museum was closed when I got there.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4661"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4662"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              VICKI
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4663"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               I, uh... 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4664"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4665"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>ON VICKI<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4666"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4667"></td><td class="line-content">     Her voice trails off. She's profoundly shaken. She knows.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4668"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4669"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              BRUCE (V.O.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4670"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Vicki? Vi --
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4671"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4672"></td><td class="line-content">     She returns the receiver to its cradle.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4673"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4674"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>ON BRUCE<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4675"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4676"></td><td class="line-content">     He hears the click. His lips part slightly. He hangs up and 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="4677"></td><td class="line-content">     sits there at the desk, staring straight ahead.

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5230"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              BRUCE

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5597"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. HELICOPTER - THAT MOMENT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5598"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5599"></td><td class="line-content">     In the bay of the helicopter stands a kid, fifteen, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5600"></td><td class="line-content">     compact, tough, and wiry: DICK GRAYSON. Like his parents, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5601"></td><td class="line-content">     he's wearing a red-and-green suit. From the copter, he's 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5602"></td><td class="line-content">     got a perfect bird's-eye view of the BATMAN-JOKER chase.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5603"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5604"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              PILOT
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5605"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Ready to go, Dick?

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5607"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              DICK
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5608"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               What's all the ruckus down there?
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5609"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5610"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>EXT. PARK - GROUND LEVEL - THAT MOMENT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5612"></td><td class="line-content">     The VAN bounces over rocks and bushes, narrowly avoiding 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5613"></td><td class="line-content">     trees, with BATMAN in hot pursuit.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5614"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5615"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. VAN - THAT MOMENT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5616"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5617"></td><td class="line-content">     At the foot of a hill, the JOKER spies a truck. On its 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5618"></td><td class="line-content">     side, in bright red letters, a WARNING: "DANGER - 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5619"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>     FIREWORKS. FLAMMABLE LOAD."

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5621"></td><td class="line-content">     The JOKER reaches into the back for a HIGHWAY FLARE.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5622"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5623"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              JOKER
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5624"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Head for the truck!

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5626"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. HELICOPTER - THAT MOMENT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5627"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5628"></td><td class="line-content">     Hovering over the chase scene, DICK catches sight of the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5629"></td><td class="line-content">     JOKER. He GASPS IN SHOCK as a LIT FLARE flies from the back 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5630"></td><td class="line-content">     of the VAN... directly into the FIREWORKS TRUCK.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5631"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5632"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>EXT. PARK - GROUND LEVEL - A MOMENT LATER<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5633"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5634"></td><td class="line-content">     THE BATMAN is thrown off his horse by the shock of a 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5635"></td><td class="line-content">     massive EXPLOSION. All at once, THE SKY IS FULL of 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5636"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>     BURSTING, INCANDESCENT COLORS!!

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5638"></td><td class="line-content">     THE JOKER hangs out of the rear of the van, looking up, an 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5639"></td><td class="line-content">     expression of PURE DELIGHT on his face.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5640"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5641"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              JOKER
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5642"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               I <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>love<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span> fireworks!

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5644"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>ANGLE ON HELICOPTERS<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5646"></td><td class="line-content">     LURCHING AND SPINNING IN THE SKY as FIREWORKS rocket past. 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5647"></td><td class="line-content">     One of them takes a dead hit on the rotor. JOHN GRAYSON 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5648"></td><td class="line-content">     falls to his death instantly; a moment later, the COPTER 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5649"></td><td class="line-content">     plummets into the trees with a resounding, fiery CRASH.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5650"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5651"></td><td class="line-content">     MARY GRAYSON hangs from the second copter as it bobs and 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5652"></td><td class="line-content">     weaves out of control. ONLOOKERS SCREAM IN TERROR.

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5654"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>EXT. STREET - THAT MOMENT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5659"></td><td class="line-content">     close to the tall buildings along the avenue.

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5676"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>ANGLE ON DICK<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5949"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. GUEST BEDROOM - THAT MOMENT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5950"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5951"></td><td class="line-content">     DICK'S BODY -- head down, feet up -- flies through the air. 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5952"></td><td class="line-content">     He SMASHES INTO a closet door and slumps to the carpet. 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5953"></td><td class="line-content">     Shaken now, and sweating profusely, he looks up at BRUCE... 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5954"></td><td class="line-content">     who stands calmly over him, adjusting his necktie.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5955"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5956"></td><td class="line-content">     A long, tense moment passes between them. Then:
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5957"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5958"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              DICK
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5959"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               ... You're <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>him<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5960"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5961"></td><td class="line-content">     No reply from BRUCE. Their gazes lock. And suddenly... 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5962"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5963"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              ALFRED (V.O.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5964"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>               FREEZE!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5965"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5966"></td><td class="line-content">     DICK and BRUCE look around. The puny, mustachioed butler 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5967"></td><td class="line-content">     stands in the doorway, feet spread in a Dirty Harry stance, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5968"></td><td class="line-content">     a .44 MAGNUM trained on DICK.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5969"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5970"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              BRUCE
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5971"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               It's all right, Alfred. Everything's
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5972"></td><td class="line-content">               under control.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5973"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5974"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              ALFRED
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5975"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               ... Very good, sir.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5976"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5977"></td><td class="line-content">     ALFRED relaxes, musters his dignity, and turns to go.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5978"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5979"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                                                 CUT TO:
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5980"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5981"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. CONFERENCE ROOM - AFTERNOON<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5982"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5983"></td><td class="line-content">     CANNED APPLAUSE as THE JOKER marches out onto a makeshift 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5984"></td><td class="line-content">     STAGE to give his QUARTERLY REPORT to the stockholders.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5985"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5986"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              JOKER
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5987"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Thankya, thankya. Ladies and germs,
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5988"></td><td class="line-content">               I'm here to tell you... we have had
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5989"></td><td class="line-content">               one <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>helluva<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span> quarter.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5990"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5991"></td><td class="line-content">     He waves a pointer at three SALES CHARTS on portable 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5992"></td><td class="line-content">     easels.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5993"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5994"></td><td class="line-content">                              JOKER (cont.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5995"></td><td class="line-content">               Panic's up. Terror's up. And fear --
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5996"></td><td class="line-content">               fear's gone straight through the
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5997"></td><td class="line-content">               <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>roof<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>. You guys should be proud --
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5998"></td><td class="line-content">               'cause I couldn'ta done it without
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="5999"></td><td class="line-content">               each and every one of you!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6000"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6001"></td><td class="line-content">     MORE CANNED APPLAUSE. The JOKER takes a bow.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6002"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6003"></td><td class="line-content">                              JOKER (cont.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6004"></td><td class="line-content">               I feel it's time to <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>expand<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span> the
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6005"></td><td class="line-content">               Joker line. I was askin' myself,
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6006"></td><td class="line-content">               what are the products that every
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6007"></td><td class="line-content">               consumer wants most? And that's when
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6008"></td><td class="line-content">               it hit me: the water you drink, and
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6009"></td><td class="line-content">               the air you breathe! Huh? Bingo!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6010"></td><td class="line-content">                     (strutting across stage)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6011"></td><td class="line-content">               Now, some of you have your eye on
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6012"></td><td class="line-content">               the profit margin. You're thinkin':
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6013"></td><td class="line-content">               this boy's too <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>ambitious<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>. You
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6014"></td><td class="line-content">               don't approve. In fact, some of you
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6015"></td><td class="line-content">               have been talking about turning me
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6016"></td><td class="line-content">               in to the cops. Or knocking me off.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6017"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6018"></td><td class="line-content">     He pauses. GLARES OUT at the audience. NO RESPONSE.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6019"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6020"></td><td class="line-content">                              JOKER (cont.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6021"></td><td class="line-content">               But that's okay. I understand. Not
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6022"></td><td class="line-content">               everyone shares my eye for beauty.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6023"></td><td class="line-content">               And just to show there's no hard
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6024"></td><td class="line-content">               feelings, I'm throwin' a little
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6025"></td><td class="line-content">               shindig tonight -- and <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>you're all<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6026"></td><td class="line-content">               <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>invited<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6027"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6028"></td><td class="line-content">     THE CANNED APPLAUSE goes right off the meter.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6029"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6030"></td><td class="line-content">                              JOKER (cont.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6031"></td><td class="line-content">               How 'bout it? IS EVERYBODY HAPPY??
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6032"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6033"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>REVERSE ANGLE - THE AUDIENCE<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6034"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6035"></td><td class="line-content">     Familiar faces all around -- the major players of the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6036"></td><td class="line-content">     Gotham underworld. But despite the enormous twisted grins, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6037"></td><td class="line-content">     no one here is laughing or applauding. No one here is
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6038"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>living<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>. The JOKER is playing to a roomful of smiling 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6039"></td><td class="line-content">     corpses.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6040"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6041"></td><td class="line-content">     One of them topples out of his chair and lands with a plop.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6042"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6043"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              JOKER
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6044"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Look at that, folks. We got 'em
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6045"></td><td class="line-content">               <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>rolling in the aisles<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>!

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6049"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. BRUCE'S BEDROOM - TOWARD DUSK<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6050"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6051"></td><td class="line-content">     VICKI lies in BRUCE's bed, under the covers, propped up on 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6052"></td><td class="line-content">     the pillows. BRUCE is in his robe over by the window, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6053"></td><td class="line-content">     looking out at his estate.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6054"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6055"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              BRUCE
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6056"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               All this apparatus, Vicki... this
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6057"></td><td class="line-content">               house, and the money, and the
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6058"></td><td class="line-content">               power... it was never mine. It was
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6059"></td><td class="line-content">               something I inherited. Bruce Wayne
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6060"></td><td class="line-content">               was something I inherited.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6061"></td><td class="line-content">                     (pause)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6062"></td><td class="line-content">               All I ever hoped for was someone who
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6063"></td><td class="line-content">               could see through Bruce -- who could
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6064"></td><td class="line-content">               see <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>me<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span> -- and not be frightened.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6065"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6066"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              VICKI
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6067"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               I'm not frightened of you, Bruce.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6068"></td><td class="line-content">               I'm frightened <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>for<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span> you.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6069"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6070"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              BRUCE

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6075"></td><td class="line-content">     she's <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>truly<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span> afraid.

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6079"></td><td class="line-content">               for me, there'd <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>be<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span> no Joker.

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6081"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                                                 CUT TO:
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6082"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6083"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. BATCAVE - EVENING<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6084"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6085"></td><td class="line-content">     TIGHT ON a tiny electronic device: two cylindrical steel 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6086"></td><td class="line-content">     casings bracketed together, topped by a DIGITAL TIMER. 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6087"></td><td class="line-content">     BRUCE makes a few adjustments with a jeweler's screwdriver, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6088"></td><td class="line-content">     hits a trigger, and watches the TIMER tick off seconds. 30. 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6089"></td><td class="line-content">     29. 28. At 25 seconds, BRUCE kills the
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6090"></td><td class="line-content">     countdown and CLAMPS THE DEVICE into an empty packet on his 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6091"></td><td class="line-content">     utility belt.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6092"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6093"></td><td class="line-content">     He stands up wearily. He's in his bat-suit, minus the cape 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6094"></td><td class="line-content">     and cowl. Behind him, hanging back discreetly in the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6095"></td><td class="line-content">     shadows, is his loyal butler ALFRED.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6096"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6097"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              BRUCE
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6098"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Where's the boy?
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6099"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6100"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              ALFRED
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6101"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Upstairs. He's quite docile.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6102"></td><td class="line-content">

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6107"></td><td class="line-content">     on tremulously.

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6111"></td><td class="line-content">               at his age.

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6113"></td><td class="line-content">                      shoulders)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6114"></td><td class="line-content">               I want you to treat him just as if
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6115"></td><td class="line-content">               he were me. Promise.

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6117"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              ALFRED
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6118"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Yes, sir.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6119"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6120"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              BRUCE

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6122"></td><td class="line-content">               Beyond that... you know what to do.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6123"></td><td class="line-content">               Don't let all this go to waste.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6124"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6125"></td><td class="line-content">     Their eyes lock for a long moment. ALFRED is unable to

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6127"></td><td class="line-content">     circular stairway which leads from the Batcave to Wayne 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6128"></td><td class="line-content">     Manor. On the third step he pauses:
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6129"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6130"></td><td class="line-content">                              BRUCE (cont.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6131"></td><td class="line-content">               Alfred? -- Thank you.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6132"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6133"></td><td class="line-content">     As BRUCE disappears up the stairs, a shaken ALFRED steadies 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6134"></td><td class="line-content">     himself against a lab table, fighting back tears.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6135"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6136"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. BRUCE'S BEDROOM - EVENING<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6137"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6138"></td><td class="line-content">     BRUCE draws the curtains, sets an alarm clock. The current 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6139"></td><td class="line-content">     time is 7:09 PM.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6140"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6141"></td><td class="line-content">     He sits cross-legged on the floor, slumps forward slightly, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6142"></td><td class="line-content">     and closes his eyes. He inhales, exhales, taking deep, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6143"></td><td class="line-content">     regular breaths. His muscles relax. Ten seconds later, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6144"></td><td class="line-content">     BRUCE has plunged into DEEP SLEEP.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6145"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6146"></td><td class="line-content">     Time passes. The clock shows 7:19, 7:32.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6147"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6148"></td><td class="line-content">     At 7:44 we TRACK IN on BRUCE's unconscious face, drawing 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6149"></td><td class="line-content">     closer and closer until HIS EYELIDS FILL THE FRAME, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6150"></td><td class="line-content">     twitching with the irregular movement characteristic of 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6151"></td><td class="line-content">     R.E.M. sleep. Without warning his EYES SNAP OPEN.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6152"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6153"></td><td class="line-content">     HOLD ON BRUCE'S GAZE -- grim, alert, determined -- as the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6154"></td><td class="line-content">     clock hits 7:45. An ALARM SOUNDS, BREAKING THE SILENCE with 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6155"></td><td class="line-content">     its grating electronic WHINE.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6156"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6157"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                                                 DISSOLVE TO:
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6158"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6159"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>EXT. ACE CHEMICAL - AERIAL SHOT - NIGHT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6160"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6161"></td><td class="line-content">     The trademark ace on the illuminated sign. From our vantage 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6162"></td><td class="line-content">     point high above, we can see THREE CARGO TRUCKS rolling out 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6163"></td><td class="line-content">     the main gates. A half-mile away, THE BATMOBILE cruises up 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6164"></td><td class="line-content">     the waterfront, approaching soundlessly, its headlights 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6165"></td><td class="line-content">     off... preparing for a final showdown with the JOKER's 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6166"></td><td class="line-content">     forces.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6167"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6168"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. ACE CHEMICAL - THAT MOMENT - NIGHT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6169"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6170"></td><td class="line-content">     The JOKER'S MINIONS, working late, readying a huge 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6171"></td><td class="line-content">     shipment. At an open loading bay, we find a DISPATCHER with 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6172"></td><td class="line-content">     a clipboard, directing MORE UNMARKED TRUCKS in the lot 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6173"></td><td class="line-content">     outside.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6174"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6175"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              DISPATCHER
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6176"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Boston, Philly: loading bay one.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6177"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6178"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>EXT. ACE CHEMICAL - THAT MOMENT - NIGHT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6179"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6180"></td><td class="line-content">     The BATMOBILE stops short of the main gate. ENGINES ROAR 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6181"></td><td class="line-content">     and the supercar ACCELERATES, SMASHING THROUGH THE GATE and 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6182"></td><td class="line-content">     taking half the chain-link fence with it.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6183"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6184"></td><td class="line-content">     In the guard's booth, ARMED GOONS pull guns as the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6185"></td><td class="line-content">     BATMOBILE streaks across the parking lot and LAUNCHES A 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6186"></td><td class="line-content">     ROCKET at the corrugated metal door which opens on the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6187"></td><td class="line-content">     factory floor. A THUNDEROUS EXPLOSION tears a gaping hole 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6188"></td><td class="line-content">     in the door.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6189"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6190"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. ACE CHEMICAL - THAT MOMENT - NIGHT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6191"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6192"></td><td class="line-content">     The BATMOBILE cruises through the flaming wreckage and 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6193"></td><td class="line-content">     SKIDS TO A HALT on the refinery floor. The JOKER'S MEN are 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6194"></td><td class="line-content">     everywhere. They take one look at the BATMOBILE, PANIC, and 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6195"></td><td class="line-content">     PELT THE CAR with a barrage of MACHINE-GUN FIRE.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6196"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6197"></td><td class="line-content">     CRACKS begin to spread across the Batmobile's plexiglass 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6198"></td><td class="line-content">     dome. Within moments, the windshield SHATTERS -- and 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6199"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>     COLLAPSES ALTOGETHER.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6200"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6201"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. BATMOBILE - THAT MOMENT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6202"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6203"></td><td class="line-content">     BULLETS rip through the upholstered passenger seats. It 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6204"></td><td class="line-content">     doesn't matter. The car is empty. <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>No one's driving<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6205"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6206"></td><td class="line-content">     TRACK IN on the computer console -- where a familiar tinny 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6207"></td><td class="line-content">     voice calmly repeats its pre-programmed command:
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6208"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6209"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              COMPUTER
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6210"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               ... Detonate.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6211"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6212"></td><td class="line-content">     A beat. Then: BLAM.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6213"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6214"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. POLICE CAR - THAT MOMENT - NIGHT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6215"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6216"></td><td class="line-content">     A CONVOY approaches Ace Chemical -- GORDON's team preparing 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6217"></td><td class="line-content">     to raid the plant. Inside each car: SPECIAL UNIT COPS 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6218"></td><td class="line-content">     dressed in asbestos suits, gas masks in their laps.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6219"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6220"></td><td class="line-content">     All at once, a BRILLIANT RED GLARE suffuses the sky.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6221"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6222"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              COP
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6223"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>                    Good Lord!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6224"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6225"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>EXT. ACE CHEMICAL - THAT MOMENT - NIGHT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6226"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6227"></td><td class="line-content">     THE JOKER'S MEN running for their lives across the parking 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6228"></td><td class="line-content">     lot, KNOCKED FLAT by the force of SIX DEAFENING EXPLOSIONS. 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6229"></td><td class="line-content">     For a few seconds everything is flame and fury. And then --
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6230"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6231"></td><td class="line-content">     All that's left of Ace Chemical is a pile of charred rubble 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6232"></td><td class="line-content">     and a PILLAR OF THICK BLACK SMOKE, spiraling up to the sky.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6233"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6234"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                                                 CUT TO:
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6235"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6236"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>EXT. ANDREWS ISLAND - NIGHT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6237"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6238"></td><td class="line-content">     DAZZLING FIREWORKS explode in the night sky over Gotham 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6239"></td><td class="line-content">     Harbor. SEARCHLIGHTS sweep across the mammoth, welcoming 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6240"></td><td class="line-content">     stone figure of LADY GOTHAM -- still wrapped in canvas, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6241"></td><td class="line-content">     ready to be unveiled.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6242"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6243"></td><td class="line-content">     THOUSANDS OF RUBBERNECKERS jam every square inch of 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6244"></td><td class="line-content">     Andrew's Island. COPS ON HORSEBACK speak into walkie-
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6245"></td><td class="line-content">     talkies as they patrol the edges of the crowd. Across the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6246"></td><td class="line-content">     Harbor, Ace Chemical is going up in flames -- but as far as 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6247"></td><td class="line-content">     the crowd can tell, with all the noise and excitement, it's 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6248"></td><td class="line-content">     just another part of the celebration.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6249"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6250"></td><td class="line-content">     At the base of the statue, GOVERNOR GILROY speaks into a 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6251"></td><td class="line-content">     microphone:
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6252"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6253"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              GOVERNOR GILROY
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6254"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               As Governor of this great state, it
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6255"></td><td class="line-content">               is now my honor to unveil for you a
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6256"></td><td class="line-content">               very special lady -- a lady who
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6257"></td><td class="line-content">               stands tall for life and liberty --
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6258"></td><td class="line-content">               America's <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>favorite<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span> lady... LADY
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6259"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>               GOTHAM!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6260"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6261"></td><td class="line-content">     The CROWD begins to APPLAUD RHYTHMICALLY, chanting 'LADY 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6262"></td><td class="line-content">     GOTHAM! LADY GOTHAM!' It's like Times Square on New Year's 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6263"></td><td class="line-content">     Eve, waiting for the big ball to drop. GILROY hoists a pair 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6264"></td><td class="line-content">     of oversized scissors and cuts a ceremonial ribbon: 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6265"></td><td class="line-content">     hydraulic CRANES kick into gear: CABLES DROP FREE, and the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6266"></td><td class="line-content">     canvas cover draws back from LADY GOTHAM's face... 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6267"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6268"></td><td class="line-content">     ... to a chorus of SCREAMS from the crowd. <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>LADY GOTHAM IS<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6269"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>WEARING A GRISLY JOKER GRIN<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>!!!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6270"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6271"></td><td class="line-content">     Suddenly -- in the midst of the hysteria -- THE 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6272"></td><td class="line-content">     SEARCHLIGHTS DIE. The STAGE LIGHTS BLINK OUT. ANDREWS 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6273"></td><td class="line-content">     ISLAND IS PLUNGED INTO DARKNESS. Instantaneous mass panic: 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6274"></td><td class="line-content">     the GOVERNOR shouts to his aides as ONLOOKERS mob the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6275"></td><td class="line-content">     stage. COPS are knocked from their horses as the CROWD 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6276"></td><td class="line-content">     stampedes. PANDEMONIUM RULES.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6277"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6278"></td><td class="line-content">     And across the harbor... block by block... GOTHAM CITY IS 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6279"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>     GOING DARK.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6280"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6281"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>EXT. GOTHAM SKIES - AERIAL SHOTS - NIGHT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6282"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6283"></td><td class="line-content">     QUICK SHOTS of FOUR HELICOPTERS hovering at different 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6284"></td><td class="line-content">     points over the blacked-out city. LOUDSPEAKERS blare out a 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6285"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>     PRE-RECORDED MESSAGE:
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6286"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6287"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              JOKER (V.O.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6288"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               HAPPY BIRTHDAY, Gotham. Here's a
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6289"></td><td class="line-content">               little token of my esteem. HAVE
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6290"></td><td class="line-content">               FUN... 'cause THE PARTY'S ON ME!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6291"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6292"></td><td class="line-content">     INSANE LAUGHTER echoes. CARGO BAYS open wide. The JOKER'S 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6293"></td><td class="line-content">     HELICOPTERS begin LEAFLETING THE CITY... with MONEY!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6294"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6295"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>SERIES OF SHOTS<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6296"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6297"></td><td class="line-content">     ANARCHY IN GOTHAM as high-denomination bills flutter to 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6298"></td><td class="line-content">     earth, blanketing the streets. HOPELESSLY OUTMANNED COPS 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6299"></td><td class="line-content">     try to maintain order as SOLID CITIZENS trample one another 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6300"></td><td class="line-content">     in a paroxysm of ANIMAL GREED. BUILDINGS EMPTY as APARTMENT 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6301"></td><td class="line-content">     DWELLERS race outside. ALL TRAFFIC STOPS as DRIVERS climb 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6302"></td><td class="line-content">     out of their cars to SNATCH MONEY FROM THE AIR.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6303"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6304"></td><td class="line-content">     DARKNESS EVERYWHERE. In the pitch-black subways, TERRIFIED 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6305"></td><td class="line-content">     COMMUTERS are seized by claustrophobia. GLASS SHATTERS, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6306"></td><td class="line-content">     DOORS BREAK OPEN as they claw their way out of stalled 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6307"></td><td class="line-content">     subway cars and SPILL OUT onto the tracks.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6308"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6309"></td><td class="line-content">     On the streets above, GOTHAM'S CRIMINAL ELEMENT is having a 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6310"></td><td class="line-content">     field day. The cops are preoccupied, utterly helpless 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6311"></td><td class="line-content">     against the first waves of RIOTING AND LOOTING.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6312"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6313"></td><td class="line-content">     FLAMES ERUPT. PUNKS race down the street carrying fur coats 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6314"></td><td class="line-content">     and color TV's. LOOTERS break through the display window of 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6315"></td><td class="line-content">     an electronics store, and climb in among the goodies... 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6316"></td><td class="line-content">     only to FLY OUT, two seconds later, on the wrong end of a 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6317"></td><td class="line-content">     SHOTGUN BLAST. <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>THE JOKER'S DREAM IS COMING TRUE<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>.

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6319"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>EXT. STREET - NIGHT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6321"></td><td class="line-content">     In a crouch on the pavement, snapping photos of the wild 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6322"></td><td class="line-content">     street action, is VICKI -- fearless, professional, <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>doing<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6323"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>her job<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>. A battered FORD ESCORT cruises up behind her.

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6325"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              KNOX
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6326"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>               VICKI!

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6352"></td><td class="line-content">     street itself, a bizarre PARADE is taking place, just as if

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6365"></td><td class="line-content">     some demented parade marshal.
