</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6491"></td><td class="line-content">     As VICKI catches up with him, KNOX drags the Batman dummy 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6492"></td><td class="line-content">     out of the store window. RIPS OFF ITS BLACK CAPE. And 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6493"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>     DASHES MANIACALLY UP THE SIDEWALK.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6494"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6495"></td><td class="line-content">     Waving the cape, he VAULTS onto the back of a SPOTLIGHT 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6496"></td><td class="line-content">     TRUCK. VICKI's face goes slack. <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>Now she gets it<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6497"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6498"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              KNOX
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6499"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>               GIMME A HAND UP HERE!

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6503"></td><td class="line-content">     assembly -- tilting the spotlight -- AIMING THE BEAM...

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6507"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. BATWING - THAT MOMENT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6513"></td><td class="line-content">     BATMAN'S MOUTH drops open. <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>He understands<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>.

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6515"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>EXT. AVENUE - ON JOKER'S FLOAT - THAT MOMENT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6516"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6517"></td><td class="line-content">     THE JOKER reaches into a big sack and begins distributing

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6520"></td><td class="line-content">     CONTROL DEVICE and points it up at the CLOWN BALLOON.

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6523"></td><td class="line-content">     bulge. Its FACE SWELLS UP as the COMPRESSOR TANK concealed 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6524"></td><td class="line-content">     inside it releases its noxious contents. The JOKER is 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6525"></td><td class="line-content">     BEAMING, a look of PURE UNALLOYED JOY on his face... 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6526"></td><td class="line-content">

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6530"></td><td class="line-content">     through the stone canyons of Gotham at a 90-degree angle to 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6531"></td><td class="line-content">     the ground!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6532"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6533"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              JOKER
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6534"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               No... NOOOOO!!!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6535"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6536"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>ANGLE ON CLOWN BALLOON<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6540"></td><td class="line-content">     now. Finally it BURSTS -- and the deadly GAS inside it 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6541"></td><td class="line-content">     disperses harmlessly in the wind.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6542"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6543"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>EXT. AVENUE - THAT MOMENT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6545"></td><td class="line-content">     THE JOKER on the edge of a tantrum as he digs amid the

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6550"></td><td class="line-content">     ... and HOWLS IN FRUSTRATION. Nothing's happening. The 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6551"></td><td class="line-content">     damned thing is <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>broken<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>. He heaves it to the street in a
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6552"></td><td class="line-content">     fit of pique.

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6560"></td><td class="line-content">     helplessly, in stunned disbelief.

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6664"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. BATWING - THAT MOMENT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6666"></td><td class="line-content">     THE BLAST all but knocks the BATWING out of the sky. BATMAN 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6667"></td><td class="line-content">     stabilizes the plane, climbs for the clouds. When he's 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6668"></td><td class="line-content">     clear of the buildings, he grits his teeth and rolls out.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6669"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6670"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>He's coming back for more<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6671"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6672"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. TANK - THAT MOMENT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6673"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6674"></td><td class="line-content">     The JOKER stares at a tiny BLIP on his radar screen.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6675"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6676"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              JOKER
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6677"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               He'll be back... he'll be back!!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6678"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6679"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>EXT. BROAD AVENUE - ON BATWING<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6680"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6681"></td><td class="line-content">     The black ultralight hurtles down Broad Avenue at full 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6682"></td><td class="line-content">     speed, on a suicide mission. MISSILES streak past on either 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6683"></td><td class="line-content">     side. MACHINE GUN FIRE peppers the dome of the cockpit. The 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6684"></td><td class="line-content">     REAR STABILIZER WING takes a direct hit... and BURSTS INTO 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6685"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>     FLAME!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6686"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6687"></td><td class="line-content">     The BATWING, trailing thick black smoke, bears down on the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6688"></td><td class="line-content">     tank like a kamikaze plane. BOMB BAYS OPEN as BATMAN dumps 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6689"></td><td class="line-content">     the last of his high explosives DIRECTLY INTO THE PATH OF 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6690"></td><td class="line-content">     THE TANK. The BATWING takes a hard bounce off the top of 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6691"></td><td class="line-content">     the tank and CRASHES TO THE STREET.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6692"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6693"></td><td class="line-content">     And suddenly a GAPING CHASM opens underneath the tank as 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6694"></td><td class="line-content">     the bombs go off -- and BROAD AVENUE BEGINS TO SPLIT WIDE 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6695"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>     OPEN!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6696"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6697"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. SUBWAY TUNNEL - THAT MOMENT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6698"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6699"></td><td class="line-content">     BROKEN CONCRETE SLABS rain down on a SUBWAY CAR stalled in 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6700"></td><td class="line-content">     the tunnel DIRECTLY BENEATH BROAD AVENUE. SUPPORT GIRDERS 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6701"></td><td class="line-content">     groan and GIVE WAY as the STREET ITSELF COLLAPSES -- and 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6702"></td><td class="line-content">     the front end of the TANK drops through, CRUSHING THE 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6703"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>     SUBWAY TRAIN BENEATH IT!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6704"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6705"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>EXT. BROAD AVENUE - THAT MOMENT - NIGHT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6706"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6707"></td><td class="line-content">     The rear end of the TANK projects out through the rubble. A 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6708"></td><td class="line-content">     hatch pops open. The JOKER crawls out through the smoke and 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6709"></td><td class="line-content">     pulls himself up to the street.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6710"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6711"></td><td class="line-content">     He's down to his last three GOONS. He points to the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6712"></td><td class="line-content">     BATWING: bent, broken, WEDGED ON ITS SIDE in the asphalt 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6713"></td><td class="line-content">     SEAM running up Broad Avenue -- half in, half out of the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6714"></td><td class="line-content">     tunnel.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6715"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6716"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              JOKER
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6717"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>You<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span> do him. I'm outta here.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6718"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6719"></td><td class="line-content">     The GOONS look on in dismay as the JOKER scurries off. They 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6720"></td><td class="line-content">     sidestep blackened debris and move up cautiously on the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6721"></td><td class="line-content">     Batwing. Through the cockpit dome they can see BATMAN... 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6722"></td><td class="line-content">     inert in his harness, beaten to a pulp, all but dead.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6723"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6724"></td><td class="line-content">     A JET OF FLAME drives them back momentarily. They reach for 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6725"></td><td class="line-content">     their guns, move in warily... 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6726"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6727"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              VOICE
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6728"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Yo.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6729"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6730"></td><td class="line-content">     The frightened GOONS turn in unison. An abrupt flurry of 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6731"></td><td class="line-content">     motion -- feet and fists flying -- quick flashes of red and 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6732"></td><td class="line-content">     green --
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6733"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6734"></td><td class="line-content">     -- and THREE GOONS lie paralyzed on the street. The only 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6735"></td><td class="line-content">     one left standing is a fifteen-year-old boy garbed in a 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6736"></td><td class="line-content">     red-and-green aerialist's uniform... DICK GRAYSON.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6737"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6738"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. BATWING - THAT MOMENT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6739"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6740"></td><td class="line-content">     BATMAN slumps at the controls. Beneath him, asphalt SHIFTS 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6741"></td><td class="line-content">     and BUCKLES. The Batwing lurches to the right, drops a foot 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6742"></td><td class="line-content">     or two into the tunnel. Metal braces collapse and the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6743"></td><td class="line-content">     plexiglass dome of the cockpit SHATTERS LIKE AN EGGSHELL.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6744"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6745"></td><td class="line-content">     TONGUES OF FIRE lick at his face. He's helpless, pinned in 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6746"></td><td class="line-content">     place. He manages to look up -- and SEES, through a dream-
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6747"></td><td class="line-content">     like haze, A HAND extended toward him:
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6748"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6749"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              DICK
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6750"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>               HEY! COME ON!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6751"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6752"></td><td class="line-content">     And suddenly DICK is clambering down into the flaming 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6753"></td><td class="line-content">     wreckage. He gets an arm around BATMAN's chest and with an 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6754"></td><td class="line-content">     extraordinary effort HAULS HIM OUT OF THE BATWING.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6755"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6756"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>EXT. STREET - A MOMENT LATER - NIGHT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6757"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6758"></td><td class="line-content">     They stagger across the ruptured street. BATMAN grimaces in 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6759"></td><td class="line-content">     agony. His right leg -- shattered -- is like rubber beneath 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6760"></td><td class="line-content">     him. His ribs are crushed. He's barely conscious.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6761"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6762"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              DICK
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6763"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Now we're even, huh? Even up.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6764"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6765"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              BATMAN
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6766"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               How did you... 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6767"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6768"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              DICK
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6769"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               I <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>hitched<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>. MOVE IT!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6770"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6771"></td><td class="line-content">     DICK drags BATMAN to safety as the Batwing ERUPTS INTO 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6772"></td><td class="line-content">     FLAME behind them.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6773"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6774"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              BATMAN
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6775"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               The Joker. Is he --?
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6776"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6777"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              DICK
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6778"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Forget it. Relax.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6779"></td><td class="line-content">                     (beat)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6780"></td><td class="line-content">               ... He's <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>mine now<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6781"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6782"></td><td class="line-content">     DICK snatches an abandoned .38 off the pavement.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6783"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6784"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              BATMAN
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6785"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>               DICK!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6786"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6787"></td><td class="line-content">     THE BATMAN tries to pull himself erect. The pain is 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6788"></td><td class="line-content">     unendurable. His body has finally failed him.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6789"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6790"></td><td class="line-content">     He collapses on the pavement, powerless to intervene, as 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6791"></td><td class="line-content">     DICK races off with murder in his eyes.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6792"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6793"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>EXT. GOTHAM CATHEDRAL - NIGHT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6794"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6795"></td><td class="line-content">     A BELLTOWER's jagged spire, jutting up into the night sky, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6796"></td><td class="line-content">     piercing the moon. Down at street level, the JOKER is 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6797"></td><td class="line-content">     scrambling up the marble steps at the entrance to the old 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6798"></td><td class="line-content">     abandoned cathedral. He pulls a WALKIE-TALKIE off his belt.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6799"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6800"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              JOKER
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6801"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Gotham cathedral. Come and get me.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6802"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6803"></td><td class="line-content">     HEAVY PANELED DOORS groan on tired hinges as THE JOKER 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6804"></td><td class="line-content">     forces his way inside. A beat. Then DICK GRAYSON appears, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6805"></td><td class="line-content">     hot on his trail, sprinting up the steps two at a time.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6806"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6807"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. CATHEDRAL - A MOMENT LATER - NIGHT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6808"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6809"></td><td class="line-content">     Ancient and creepy. A huge pipe organ, shattered stained
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6810"></td><td class="line-content">     glass windows, row after row of mahogany pews... all 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6811"></td><td class="line-content">     forgotten, covered with dust and cobwebs. The JOKER wanders 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6812"></td><td class="line-content">     about, staring at the statuary, the rusted icons.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6813"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6814"></td><td class="line-content">     DICK enters silently behind him. He kneels behind a rear 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6815"></td><td class="line-content">     pew, brings up the gun, and squeezes off THREE QUICK SHOTS 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6816"></td><td class="line-content">     at the JOKER. The JOKER dives, takes cover, and RETURNS 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6817"></td><td class="line-content">     DICK'S FIRE. Then: silence.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6818"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6819"></td><td class="line-content">     In a crouch, groping his way along the wall, THE JOKER 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6820"></td><td class="line-content">     finds what he wants: a small door opening on a wooden 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6821"></td><td class="line-content">     stairway, leading to the belltower. He ducks inside and 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6822"></td><td class="line-content">     starts up.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6823"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6824"></td><td class="line-content">     DICK'S GUN drops with a thud. His hand slips from the back 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6825"></td><td class="line-content">     of the pew. In the second before he slumps to the floor, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6826"></td><td class="line-content">     unconscious, he sees a curious sight: a TINY BLACK NINJA 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6827"></td><td class="line-content">     WHEEL, imbedded in the flesh of his leg.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6828"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6829"></td><td class="line-content">     Behind him -- framed in the arched doorway -- A RAGGED 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6830"></td><td class="line-content">     BLACK GHOST begins his final unholy march down the center 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6831"></td><td class="line-content">     aisle of the old cathedral.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6832"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6833"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. CATHEDRAL - BELLTOWER - NIGHT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6834"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6835"></td><td class="line-content">     A tiny stone chamber, 8'x8', open on four sides to the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6836"></td><td class="line-content">     wind. The enormous church bell has long since been removed.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6837"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6838"></td><td class="line-content">     The JOKER stands in an archway, gazing at the gargoyles on 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6839"></td><td class="line-content">     the roof below. He hits a button on the walkie-talkie:
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6840"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6841"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              JOKER
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6842"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               I'm in the belltower. Don't land.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6843"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6844"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. HELICOPTER - MOVING - NIGHT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6845"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6846"></td><td class="line-content">     A PILOT replies through his radio headset.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6847"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6848"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              PILOT
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6849"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               E.T.A. two minutes. Hang on.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6850"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6851"></td><td class="line-content">     The PILOT swings the copter right in a wide, swooping arc.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6852"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6853"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. STAIRWAY TO BELLTOWER - THAT MOMENT - NIGHT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6854"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6855"></td><td class="line-content">     BATMAN. Broken, beaten, his right leg useless, he hauls 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6856"></td><td class="line-content">     himself up the steps one at a time. <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>He should be dead<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6857"></td><td class="line-content">     Dried blood cakes his face, his chest.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6858"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6859"></td><td class="line-content">     Dizzy, exhausted, his body strained to the limit, he slumps 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6860"></td><td class="line-content">     against a wall to steady himself, then reaches into his 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6861"></td><td class="line-content">     utility belt for a painkiller -- and forces the capsule 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6862"></td><td class="line-content">     back onto his dry, swollen tongue.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6863"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6864"></td><td class="line-content">     Quaking all over, he tries to draw himself erect... and 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6865"></td><td class="line-content">     TOPPLES OVER, landing with his full weight on the rotten 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6866"></td><td class="line-content">     wood of the belltower stairs.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6867"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6868"></td><td class="line-content">     THE STAIRWAY COLLAPSES, turning to splinters beneath him. 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6869"></td><td class="line-content">     And suddenly BATMAN finds himself DANGLING PRECARIOUSLY IN 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6870"></td><td class="line-content">     MIDAIR, hanging by one hand to an upper step.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6871"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6872"></td><td class="line-content">     It would be so much easier to let go. He looks down at the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6873"></td><td class="line-content">     fragments of the shattered stairway, STILL FALLING, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6874"></td><td class="line-content">     vanishing into the dark depths of the stairwell.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6875"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6876"></td><td class="line-content">     Then he looks up. At the trapdoor. A mere six feet away. 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6877"></td><td class="line-content">     His TEETH CLENCH in a monstrous grimace. AND WITH AN 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6878"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>     INHUMAN EFFORT, HE HOISTS HIMSELF UP ONTO THE UPPER STEPS.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6879"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6880"></td><td class="line-content">     For a full five seconds he's blind with pain. A RAGGED 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6881"></td><td class="line-content">     WOODEN SHAFT is buried in his right shoulder. Twitching, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6882"></td><td class="line-content">     trembling, he reaches up and YANKS IT OUT with his last 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6883"></td><td class="line-content">     ounce of strength.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6884"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6885"></td><td class="line-content">     The trapdoor is a foot above his head. It could be a mile. 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6886"></td><td class="line-content">     BATMAN finally realizes he's not going to make it.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6887"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6888"></td><td class="line-content">     He reaches down and rips open a Velcro seal on his utility 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6889"></td><td class="line-content">     belt, revealing the strange TIMER DEVICE we saw him making 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6890"></td><td class="line-content">     earlier. Before he can activate it his hand falls limply at 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6891"></td><td class="line-content">     his side.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6892"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6893"></td><td class="line-content">     THE BATMAN is out like a light.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6894"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6895"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. BELLTOWER - THAT MOMENT - NIGHT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6896"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6897"></td><td class="line-content">     The JOKER glances casually down at the trapdoor, wondering 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6898"></td><td class="line-content">     what all the noise is about. He draws his gun, moves 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6899"></td><td class="line-content">     cautiously to the trapdoor, and lifts it a few inches... 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6900"></td><td class="line-content">     just enough to see the unconscious form on the stairs.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6901"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6902"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              JOKER
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6903"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               ... Batman?
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6904"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6905"></td><td class="line-content">     No reply. The JOKER stands there and lets out a little 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6906"></td><td class="line-content">     snicker. He looks out through the archway, sees no sign of 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6907"></td><td class="line-content">     his rescue copter. Then -- a look of curious amusement on 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6908"></td><td class="line-content">     his face -- he steps down THROUGH THE TRAPDOOR and LUGS 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6909"></td><td class="line-content">     BATMAN up into the belltower.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6910"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6911"></td><td class="line-content">     He props BATMAN up against a wall. Still no sign of life. 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6912"></td><td class="line-content">     The JOKER crouches beside him and -- almost tenderly -- 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6913"></td><td class="line-content">     pats his face.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6914"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6915"></td><td class="line-content">                              JOKER (cont.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6916"></td><td class="line-content">               Batman? Batman?
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6917"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6918"></td><td class="line-content">     THE BATMAN's lips part. But he's too weak to speak.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6919"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6920"></td><td class="line-content">                              JOKER (cont.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6921"></td><td class="line-content">               I thought you'd be more comfortable
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6922"></td><td class="line-content">               here in the belfry.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6923"></td><td class="line-content">                     (chuckling to himself)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6924"></td><td class="line-content">               Before I kill you I'd like to see
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6925"></td><td class="line-content">               who you are. Would that be okay?
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6926"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6927"></td><td class="line-content">     BATMAN emits a tiny low moan. The JOKER takes it as a yes 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6928"></td><td class="line-content">     and reaches over to undo his cowl.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6929"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6930"></td><td class="line-content">     BRUCE WAYNE stares up with dulled, sightless eyes. The 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6931"></td><td class="line-content">     JOKER reaches into his pocket for a purple handkerchief, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6932"></td><td class="line-content">     moistens it, dabs at the caked blood on BRUCE's face.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6933"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6934"></td><td class="line-content">                              JOKER (cont.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6935"></td><td class="line-content">               Oh my, aren't we pretty.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6936"></td><td class="line-content">                     (brightening suddenly)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6937"></td><td class="line-content">               I know you! You're the rich boy!!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6938"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6939"></td><td class="line-content">     The JOKER is enormously tickled by this discovery. He claps 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6940"></td><td class="line-content">     his hands together in sheer glee.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6941"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6942"></td><td class="line-content">                              JOKER (cont.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6943"></td><td class="line-content">               My goodness, what in the world made
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6944"></td><td class="line-content">               you <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>do it<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>? It must've been
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6945"></td><td class="line-content">               something pretty terrible!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6946"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6947"></td><td class="line-content">     He's practically dancing now. He's made a friend.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6948"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6949"></td><td class="line-content">                              JOKER (cont.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6950"></td><td class="line-content">               You know, we should've sat down and
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6951"></td><td class="line-content">               had us a little heart-to-heart. I
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6952"></td><td class="line-content">               bet we would have got on famously.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6953"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6954"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              BATMAN
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6955"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Mad... man... 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6956"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6957"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              JOKER
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6958"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Well now, you're not exactly the
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6959"></td><td class="line-content">               picture of mental health, are you.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6960"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6961"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              BATMAN
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6962"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               ... Murderer... 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6963"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6964"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              JOKER
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6965"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               Bruce, we're both murderers. Think
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6966"></td><td class="line-content">               how many people you've killed by
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6967"></td><td class="line-content">               letting me live.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6968"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6969"></td><td class="line-content">     A SPOTLIGHT cuts through the night sky. The JOKER hears his 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6970"></td><td class="line-content">     helicopter approaching in the distance.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6971"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6972"></td><td class="line-content">     BRUCE reaches down furtively. Finds the timer on his 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6973"></td><td class="line-content">     utility belt. FLICKS A SWITCH... and the countdown begins.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6974"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6975"></td><td class="line-content">     The JOKER pulls a straight razor from his pocket and opens 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6976"></td><td class="line-content">     it gingerly.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6977"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6978"></td><td class="line-content">                              JOKER (cont.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6979"></td><td class="line-content">               I have to do it now, Bruce, but it
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6980"></td><td class="line-content">               won't even hurt. Now relax. The
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6981"></td><td class="line-content">               bat's in his belfry, all's right
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6982"></td><td class="line-content">               with the world... 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6983"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6984"></td><td class="line-content">     He has the razor almost up to BRUCE's throat when BRUCE 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6985"></td><td class="line-content">     reaches out and GRABS HIS LAPELS in a death grip. The JOKER 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6986"></td><td class="line-content">     is momentarily amused by this seeming display of affection.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6987"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6988"></td><td class="line-content">                              JOKER (cont.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6989"></td><td class="line-content">               Why, <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>Bruce<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>... 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6990"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6991"></td><td class="line-content">     Then he hears ticking.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6992"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6993"></td><td class="line-content">     Looks down at the flashing digital display on BRUCE's belt. 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6994"></td><td class="line-content">     0:26 seconds. 0:25 seconds.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6995"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6996"></td><td class="line-content">     He SHRIEKS HORRIFICALLY and DROPS THE RAZOR.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6997"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6998"></td><td class="line-content">     BRUCE won't let go of him. Finally he manages to lurch 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="6999"></td><td class="line-content">     convulsively away, sprawling on the floor of the belfry.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7000"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7001"></td><td class="line-content">     BRUCE is wearing a great big Joker smile.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7002"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7003"></td><td class="line-content">                              JOKER (cont.)
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7004"></td><td class="line-content">               <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>IT'S NOT FUNNY<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>!!!
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7005"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7006"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              BRUCE
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7007"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>               No... sense... of humor?
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7008"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7009"></td><td class="line-content">     The JOKER reaches out for the ticking time bomb. Thinks 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7010"></td><td class="line-content">     better of it and retracts his shaking hand.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7011"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7012"></td><td class="line-content">     He can see the copter approaching now, slicing through the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7013"></td><td class="line-content">     clouds. He screams, waves a flashlight in the air: his 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7014"></td><td class="line-content">     signal beacon. 0:20 and counting.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7015"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7016"></td><td class="line-content">     The JOKER scans the belltower frantically. His eyes fall on 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7017"></td><td class="line-content">     the trapdoor. He races over, flings it open, starts down 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7018"></td><td class="line-content">     the stairs in a frenzy.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7019"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7020"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>There are no stairs<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>. They've collapsed. 0:16 and 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7021"></td><td class="line-content">     counting.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7022"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7023"></td><td class="line-content">     Screaming insanely, the JOKER vaults through the door and 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7024"></td><td class="line-content">     makes for the open stone archway. The copter is directly 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7025"></td><td class="line-content">     overhead now. A rope ladder drops from its belly.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7026"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7027"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>EXT. BELLTOWER - THAT MOMENT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7028"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7029"></td><td class="line-content">     The helicopter descends, its whirling blades stirring up a 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7030"></td><td class="line-content">     windstorm on the roof of the old abandoned cathedral. DEAD 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7031"></td><td class="line-content">     LEAVES rise and swirl in the churning air.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7032"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7033"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. BELLTOWER<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7034"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7035"></td><td class="line-content">     The JOKER makes a futile grab at the rope ladder, almost 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7036"></td><td class="line-content">     losing his purchase on the archway parapet. He gestures 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7037"></td><td class="line-content">     wildly for the copter to make another pass. 0:12 to go.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7038"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7039"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>EXT. BELLTOWER<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7040"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7041"></td><td class="line-content">     A maelstrom of swirling leaves. And now, among the leaves 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7042"></td><td class="line-content">     -- roused from their resting place in the rotten rafters of 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7043"></td><td class="line-content">     the old cathedral --
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7044"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7045"></td><td class="line-content">     -- A HORDE OF SQUEALING, CHITTERING <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>BATS<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>!! Filling the air 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7046"></td><td class="line-content">     like a black cloud, <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>HUNDREDS OF THEM<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>, taking flight in
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7047"></td><td class="line-content">     blind uncomprehending fury --
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7048"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7049"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. BELLTOWER<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7050"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7051"></td><td class="line-content">     The JOKER leaps into empty space, grabs hold of the ladder, 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7052"></td><td class="line-content">     cackles in mad triumph --
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7053"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7054"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>     -- AND SUDDENLY THE BELLTOWER IS FULL OF BATS. A SCREECHING 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7055"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>     SWARM, HIDEOUS, BLACK-WINGED -- SWOOPING THROUGH THE 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7056"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>     ARCHWAYS <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>DIRECTLY AT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span> THE JOKER --

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7058"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>     -- WHO SCREAMS IN TERROR -- LETS GO OF THE LADDER --
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7059"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7060"></td><td class="line-content">     -- and plunges into the night.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7061"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7062"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>TIGHT ON BATMAN<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>. Six seconds remain. <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>There is still time<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span> if 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7063"></td><td class="line-content">     he makes his choice now.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7064"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7065"></td><td class="line-content">     Surrounded by the flapping of leathery wings, his body 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7066"></td><td class="line-content">     working on pure adrenalin, he unbuckles the belt. Lurches 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7067"></td><td class="line-content">     into position. Heaves it out into the darkness.

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7069"></td><td class="line-content">     It snags on the bottom rung of the dangling rope ladder.

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7071"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>INT. HELICOPTER - POV CO-PILOT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7073"></td><td class="line-content">     The CO-PILOT is hanging out one side of the copter, just 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7074"></td><td class="line-content">     enough to see what's going on.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7075"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7076"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              CO-PILOT
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7077"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>               PULL UP!! PULL --

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7079"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>EXT. CHURCHYARD - OVERHEAD ANGLE<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7080"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7081"></td><td class="line-content">     It's as if time has stopped. The world has grown suddenly 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7082"></td><td class="line-content">     silent. We're looking down at the JOKER, whose body lies 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7083"></td><td class="line-content">     splayed and broken on the flagstone surface of the 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7084"></td><td class="line-content">     churchyard. Slowly, elegantly -- we have all the time in 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7085"></td><td class="line-content">     the world, now -- we DRIFT DOWNWARD, closer, until his FACE 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7086"></td><td class="line-content">     FILLS THE SCREEN, the familiar chilling grin still intact.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7087"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7088"></td><td class="line-content">     Sad clown, A-one crazy boy, staring aimlessly at the stars. 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7089"></td><td class="line-content">     Suddenly his face is bathed in a brilliant gasoline GLOW.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7090"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7091"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>POV JOKER<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7093"></td><td class="line-content">     Looking up he sees a beautiful display of fireworks,

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7097"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>REVERSE ANGLE - THE JOKER'S FACE<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7098"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7099"></td><td class="line-content">     It's all so lovely. The JOKER's expression is happy, almost 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7100"></td><td class="line-content">     childlike, as he gazes up at this private show. Gradually,

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7109"></td><td class="line-content">     AN ANCHORWOMAN delivering an oncamera EDITORIAL.
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7110"></td><td class="line-content">
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7111"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>                              ANCHORWOMAN

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7195"></td><td class="line-content">     rings on his way down.

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7202"></td><td class="line-content">     <span class="html-tag">&lt;u&gt;</span>EXT. ROOFTOP - GOTHAM CITY - NIGHT<span class="html-tag">&lt;/u&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7203"></td><td class="line-content">

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7205"></td><td class="line-content">     distance. CAMERA DRIFTS across the rooftop, settling

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7207"></td><td class="line-content">     the edge of the roof, gazing down on the streets below.

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7209"></td><td class="line-content">     A SECOND FIGURE enters frame. We get a brief glimpse of his 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7210"></td><td class="line-content">     RED-AND-GREEN SUIT in the seconds before our EYES TURN 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7211"></td><td class="line-content">     SKYWARD... to the SEARING YELLOW SPOTLIGHT sweeping through 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7212"></td><td class="line-content">     the clouds. In its center: the VAST BLACK SILHOUETTE of a 
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7213"></td><td class="line-content">     BAT, wings extended, DOMINATING the night sky.

</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7220"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>
</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="7221"></td><td class="line-content">
